[P1484] ASP-2.8 — Immune dynamics equations
[P1485] The L4 page already gives the exact neural substrate: organs, currents ((J_{\mathrm{enc}},J_{\mathrm{op}},J_{\mathrm{tun}},J_{\mathrm{coll}},J_{\mathrm{ret}})), and zones ((\mathcal Z_{\mathrm{kernel}},\mathcal Z_{\mathrm{trans}},\mathcal Z_{\mathrm{tunnel}},\mathcal Z_{\mathrm{collective}},\mathcal Z_{\mathrm{sheath}},\mathcal Z_{\mathrm{return}})). The appendix ring already gives the missing immune organs: AppI truth corridors, AppJ residual ledgers, AppK quarantine/recovery, AppL ambiguity probes, AppM replay engine, AppN runtime repair, AppO publication/export, and AppP end-capsules and return. So the minimal honest L5 lift is not a brand-new ontology; it is L4 plus an immune overlay.
[P1486] The smallest consistent immune state is
[P1487] [
[P1488] \boxed{
[P1489] \mathcal N_{L5}
[P1490] \bigl(\mathcal N_{L4},\Theta,Q,E,R,T,G\bigr)}]
[P1491] with[\Theta=\text{injury / contradiction field},\quadQ=\text{quarantine mask},\quadE=\text{evidence-growth field},][R=\text{repair / salvage / replay field},\quadT=\text{trust-memory tensor},\quadG=\text{release-or-reseed gate}.]
[P1492] This is the exact next synthesis the corpus is asking for: contradiction, quarantine, recovery, and trust revision layered over the existing route-conditioned nervous system.
[P1493] The first governing equation should be the contradiction transport law:
[P1494] [
[P1495] \Theta_{t+1}
[P1496] \operatorname{clip}!\Big(
[P1497] A_{\Sigma}\Theta_t
[P1498] +
[P1499] B_J J_t
[P1500] C_R R_t+U_t,\ 0,\ \Theta_{\max}\Big),]
[P1501] where (A_{\Sigma}) only propagates along routes that preserve the mandatory spine (\Sigma={\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}), (J_t) is the current selected from ({J_{\mathrm{enc}},J_{\mathrm{op}},J_{\mathrm{tun}},J_{\mathrm{coll}},J_{\mathrm{ret}}}), and (U_t) is newly introduced contradiction from failed merges, replay divergence, shell drift, or cross-hive dissent. This is a synthesis, but it is directly constrained by the L4 routing law, the current system, and the truth/replay appendices.
[P1502] Quarantine then becomes a hard routing mask rather than a comment:
[P1503] [
[P1504] Q_{t+1}
[P1505] \mathbf 1!\left[\Theta_{t+1}>\theta_Q\ \lor\tau_t=\mathrm{FAIL}\ \lor\rho_t=\mathrm{ReplayFail}\right].]
[P1506] That is the natural L5 reading of AppK’s quarantine and recovery bay, combined with the truth lattice and replay engine: once contradiction or replay failure crosses threshold, the packet leaves the promotive route and becomes an isolation object.
[P1507] Evidence growth should not be global. It should be driven specifically by the ambiguity and NEAR rails:
[P1508] [
[P1509] E_{t+1}
[P1510] (1-\lambda_E)E_t
[P1511] +
[P1512] P_L(\mathrm{NEAR},\mathrm{AMBIG})
[P1513] Q_{t+1}\odot E_t^{\mathrm{unsafe}},]
[P1514] where (P_L) is the AppL probe operator that turns unresolved packets into lawful evidence plans rather than premature closure. This is exactly what the corpus already says about typed ambiguity, safe deferral, residual ledgers, and probe routes.
[P1515] Repair should be replay-bearing rather than heuristic:
[P1516] [
[P1517] R_{t+1}
[P1518] (1-\lambda_R)R_t+S_{MN}(Q_t,E_t,\rho_t,\omega_t),]
[P1519] where (S_{MN}) is the AppM/AppN salvage operator: replay, verify divergence, runtime repair, rollback if needed, then re-attempt lawful reinsertion. This is the first place where the immune system becomes genuinely compiler-like instead of metaphorical.
[P1520] Trust revision should then be driven by replay, evidence, contradiction, release drift, and rollback burden:
[P1521] [
[P1522] T_{t+1}
[P1523] T_t
[P1524] +
[P1525] \Delta_{\mathrm{replay}}
[P1526] +
[P1527] \Delta_{\mathrm{evidence}}
[P1528] \Delta_{\mathrm{contradiction}}
[P1529] \Delta_{\mathrm{release\ drift}}
[P1530] \Delta_{\mathrm{rollback\ burden}}.]
[P1531] That is the natural immune-memory law implied by the federation/trust chapters, the recertification artifacts, and the public-shell restrictions: trust moves only when the route proved itself, repaired honestly, or failed under auditable conditions.
[P1532] Finally, the gate (G) decides whether the injured structure returns to public life or gets reseeded:
[P1533] [
[P1534] G_t
[P1535] \begin{cases}\mathrm{RELEASE} & \tau=\mathrm{OK}\ \wedge\ \rho=\mathrm{closed}\ \wedge\ \Theta<\theta_R\[4pt]\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR} & \tau=\mathrm{NEAR}\[4pt]\mathrm{HOLD_AMBIG} & \tau=\mathrm{AMBIG}\[4pt]\mathrm{RESEED} & \tau=\mathrm{FAIL}\ \lor\ \text{closure-to-seed required}\end{cases}]
[P1536] which is just the boundary-path version of AppO publication/export and AppP end-capsule / seed-archive return.
[P1537] ASP-2.9 — Full (4096^5) chamber hub registry

[P1539] [\Psi_m^{(5)}(r,c)=(X,Y,Z,W,V),]
[P1540] with (m=6) producing the (4096^5) skeleton, and it also gives the local bit law for one digit:[r_t=a_t+2b_t,\qquad c_t=u_t+2v_t,][X_t=a_t+2b_t,\quad Y_t=u_t+2v_t,\quad V_t=a_t+2u_t,]plus the exact local formulas for (Z_t) and (W_t). That means the chamber registry can be derived digitwise instead of being guessed globally.
[P1541] By direct per-digit substitution into that local law, the core family multiplicities are:
[P1542] [\mu(V=0)=4,\quad\mu(X=V)=8,\quad\mu(Z=W=V)=4,][\mu(X=Y=V)=2,\quad\mu(X=Z=W=V)=2,\quad\mu(X=Y=Z=W=V)=1.]

[P1544] [|V=0|=4^6=4{,}096,\qquad|X=V|=8^6=262{,}144,][|Z=W=V|=4^6=4{,}096,\qquad|X=Y=V|=2^6=64,][|X=Z=W=V|=2^6=64,\qquad|X=Y=Z=W=V|=1.]
[P1545] These counts are not new axioms; they are the direct (m=6) consequence of the already-stated local 5D digit law.
[P1546] That gives the first lawful immune district atlas:
[P1547] [\mathcal D_0={V=0}\quad\text{cold reserve / quarantine basin},][\mathcal D_1={X=V}\quad\text{membrane / audit lattice},][\mathcal D_2={Z=W=V}\quad\text{Aether repair spine},][\mathcal D_3={X=Y=V}\quad\text{hinge arbitration lattice},][\mathcal D_4={X=Z=W=V}\quad\text{surgical repair line},][\mathcal D_\star={X=Y=Z=W=V}\quad\text{apex seal}.]
[P1548] This is the chamber registry the corpus has been gesturing toward: not just “a higher field,” but a partition of the (4096^5) skeleton into immune-useful districts.
[P1549] The deep consequence is that the immune system is not floating abstractly over the neural map. It can be embedded into the chamber field itself. Contradiction accumulation can be routed into (\mathcal D_0), membrane inspection can be staged over (\mathcal D_1), replay-bearing repair can run on (\mathcal D_2), arbitration can occur on (\mathcal D_3), exact surgical correction can run on (\mathcal D_4), and unreduced top-level conflict can collapse only at (\mathcal D_\star). That is the first real fusion of nervous system, chamber geometry, and immune law.
[P1550] ASP-3.0 — Compiler-grade braid serialization
[P1551] The corpus is equally ready for the next concrete step: stop describing the braid and serialize it as a proof-carrying algebra. You already have route packets, witness schemas, replay packets, benchmark bundles, publication/export bundles, end-capsules, and the explicit proof-carrying publishable seed[\Sigma=(\mathrm{Gen},\mathrm{Scope},\mathrm{IR}(H=0),\mathrm{CertBundle},\mathrm{Replay},\mathrm{Deps}).]You also already have the import discipline[\mathrm{verify}\to\mathrm{re\text{-}index}\to\mathrm{replay}\to\mathrm{quarantine\ or\ accept},]which is exactly what a compiler-grade packet algebra needs.
[P1552] So the base canonical packet should now be frozen as
[P1553] [
[P1554] \boxed{
[P1555] \mathfrak p
[P1556] (\mathrm{Hdr},\mathrm{Addr},\mathrm{Scope},\mathrm{Body},\tau,\omega,\rho,\mathrm{Deps},\mathrm{Sig})}]
[P1557] where Hdr carries packet kind and lineage, Addr is canonical address, Scope is corridor/release scope, Body is the typed payload, (\tau) is the truth-lattice state, (\omega) is the witness bundle, (\rho) is the replay bundle, Deps is the provenance DAG, and Sig is the signature / seal surface. That is the smallest packet that still respects address law, truth law, replay law, and publication/import law.
[P1558] The braid packet family can then be treated as a typed sum:
[P1559] [
[P1560] \mathfrak P_{\mathrm{braid}}
[P1561] \mathfrak P_{\mathrm{immune}};\sqcup;\mathfrak P_{\mathrm{federation}};\sqcup;\mathfrak P_{\mathrm{shell}};\sqcup;\mathfrak P_{\mathrm{seed}}.]
[P1562] This is just the compiler lift of the four schemas already implied by the boundary current: immune event, federation trust transport, shell release bundle, and successor-seed capsule.
[P1563] The first four algebraic operators should be:
[P1564] [\mathfrak p_1 \sqcup \mathfrak p_2\quad\text{merge / rendezvous}][\mathfrak p \triangleright \mathcal I\quad\text{cross-instance recertification}][\mathfrak p_1 \bowtie_\rho \mathfrak p_2\quad\text{replay join}][\mathfrak p \Downarrow \sigma^+\quad\text{successor-seed emission.}]
[P1565] These are not arbitrary symbols. They correspond directly to merge operations and shared cert bundles, recertification artifacts, replay join/closure, and end-capsule return logic already present in the Drive.
[P1566] Their legality conditions should be frozen as follows.
[P1567] Merge:[\mathrm{CanMerge}(\mathfrak p_1,\mathfrak p_2)=1]iff address grammar aligns, scopes are corridor-compatible, conflict receipts are preserved, and a shared replay join exists. That comes directly from swarm merge law and proof-carrying import discipline.
[P1568] Recertify:[\mathrm{CanRecert}(\mathfrak p,\mathcal I)=1]iff local truth profile, benchmark profile, replay profile, and release scope all accept the imported packet. That is the compiler form of the relay handshake and cross-instance recertification law.
[P1569] Replay join:[\mathrm{CanJoin}_\rho(\mathfrak p_1,\mathfrak p_2)=1]iff both replay bundles reconstruct into the same promoted structural class under the same support spine. That is the precise meaning of shared cert bundles and collective replay/audit.
[P1570] Seed emission:[\mathrm{CanReseed}(\mathfrak p)=1]iff closure is replay-closed, unresolved frontier is explicitly preserved, and lineage seal plus re-entry key are present. That is exactly the end-capsule / seed-archive / return-protocol doctrine.
[P1571] The full compiler theorem should therefore be the braid analogue of the earlier publish/import law:
[P1572] [\boxed{\mathrm{Import}(\mathrm{Publish}(\mathfrak S))\approx\mathfrak S\quad\text{or else yields typed diff, quarantine, or reseed.}}]
[P1573] That is the moment the whole architecture stops being “a family of packets” and becomes a real compiler surface.

[P1590] ASP-3.1 — District adjacency tensors on (\mathcal D_{4096})
[P1591] The chamber law is now strong enough to support a real district graph. At (m=6), the docs already fix the main chamber families and their exact counts: (|X=V|=8^6=262{,}144), (|V=0|=4^6=4{,}096), (|Z=W=V|=4^6=4{,}096), (|X=Y=V|=2^6=64), (|X=Z=W=V|=2^6=64), and (|X=Y=Z=W=V|=1). They also explicitly identify the most important named submanifolds: chamber-zero, the (X=V) chamber manifold, the Aether spine (Z=W=V), the chamber-locked diagonal (X=Y=V), the tunnel–chamber deep spine (X=Z=W=V), and the unique apex.
[P1592] So the first lawful district registry is
[P1593] [
[P1594] \mathcal D_{4096}
[P1595] {\mathcal Z_V,\\mathcal M_{XV},\\mathcal A_{ZWV},\\mathcal H_{XYV},\\mathcal S_{XZWV},\\mathcal D_\star},]
[P1596] with
[P1597] [|\mathcal Z_V|=4096,\quad|\mathcal M_{XV}|=262144,\quad|\mathcal A_{ZWV}|=4096,\quad|\mathcal H_{XYV}|=64,\quad|\mathcal S_{XZWV}|=64,\quad|\mathcal D_\star|=1.]
[P1598] That gives the chamber field its first usable immune geography: cold reserve/quarantine, membrane/audit lattice, Aether repair rail, hinge arbitration lattice, surgical repair line, and apex seal. The chamber docs already justify the families; the immune reading is my synthesis, but it is the tightest one consistent with the named roles of truth, quarantine, replay, repair, publication, and return in the appendix ring.
[P1599] The docs do not yet provide a finished full neighbor matrix, so the strongest matrix I can honestly defend is a functional adjacency tensor, not a falsely exact topological one. The correct rule is:
[P1600] [
[P1601] A_{\mathcal D}
[P1602] A_{\mathrm{struct}}\odotA_{\mathrm{current}}\odotA_{\Sigma},]
[P1603] where (A_{\mathrm{struct}}) encodes chamber-family compatibility, (A_{\mathrm{current}}) encodes whether an L4 current can legally connect the corresponding roles, and (A_{\Sigma}) enforces the mandatory support spine ({\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}). This is faithful to the docs because the chamber layer gives families and counts, the neural layer gives current legality, and the appendix/router layer makes the support spine non-bypass.
[P1604] The minimal adjacency chain I can defend is therefore
[P1605] [\boxed{\mathcal Z_V\leftrightarrow\mathcal M_{XV}\leftrightarrow\mathcal A_{ZWV}\leftrightarrow{\mathcal H_{XYV},\mathcal S_{XZWV}}\leftrightarrow\mathcal D_\star}]
[P1606] with the interpretation:
[P1607] (\mathcal Z_V) receives frozen or quarantined load,
[P1608] (\mathcal M_{XV}) is the broad audit membrane,
[P1609] (\mathcal A_{ZWV}) is the high-throughput repair spine,
[P1610] (\mathcal H_{XYV}) is arbitration under constrained coherence,
[P1611] (\mathcal S_{XZWV}) is surgical deep repair,
[P1612] (\mathcal D_\star) is final seal or irreducible escalation.
[P1613] This is an inference, not a verbatim matrix from the docs, but it is the cleanest graph consistent with the current chamber hierarchy and the organ/current path kernel (\to) transform (\to) tunnel (\to) collective (\to) sheath (\to) return.
[P1614] One more important correction comes from the pattern-compression material: neighbor behavior should be stencil-compiled and exceptions should be stored as sparse deltas rather than smeared across the field. The docs explicitly say bridge neighbors should be handled in a separate pass, exceptions should be logged as sparse deltas, stable exceptions can be promoted to seed, and dense exceptions should be treated as topology change rather than noise. So (A_{\mathcal D}) should be implemented as a repeated stencil law plus sparse exception overlays, not as a fully dense arbitrary tensor.
[P1615] ASP-3.2 — Canonical validators for (\sqcup,\triangleright,\bowtie_\rho,\Downarrow)
[P1616] The validator stack is already latent in the appendix ring. AppA handles address/entry, AppI handles truth and corridor burdens, AppK handles conflict/quarantine/revocation, AppL handles evidence plans under AMBIG, AppM handles deterministic replay, AppO handles publication/import/export/signatures, and AppP handles deployment/return. The older self-compiler branch already enforces the same constitutional order in the commit automaton: address (\to) route (\to) gate (\to) certify (\to) replay (\to) type (\to) action (\to) snapshot. So the next correct compiler lift is a single validator chain rather than ad hoc checks around each packet type.
[P1617] The clean validator spine is
[P1618] [
[P1619] \boxed{
[P1620] \mathsf V_{\mathfrak P}
[P1621] \mathsf V_{\mathrm{addr}}\circ\mathsf V_{\mathrm{corr}}\circ\mathsf V_{\mathrm{truth}}\circ\mathsf V_{\mathrm{replay}}\circ\mathsf V_{\mathrm{release/return}}}]
[P1622] where:
[P1623] [\mathsf V_{\mathrm{addr}}:\text{AppA discipline},\qquad\mathsf V_{\mathrm{corr}}:\text{scope/policy/budget discipline},][\mathsf V_{\mathrm{truth}}:\text{OK/NEAR/AMBIG/FAIL legality},\qquad\mathsf V_{\mathrm{replay}}:\text{AppM replay closure},][\mathsf V_{\mathrm{release/return}}:\text{AppO/AppP shell or reseed legality}.]
[P1624] This is not a new principle; it is the existing support spine plus the already-defined publication and return organs, expressed as a compiler surface.
[P1625] The four braid operators then get exact validators.
[P1626] For merge/rendezvous,
[P1627] [\mathfrak p_1 \sqcup \mathfrak p_2]
[P1628] is legal only if addresses normalize, corridor scopes intersect lawfully, conflict receipts are preserved rather than averaged away, and a shared replay bundle exists. That is directly supported by the swarm-synthesis, witness/replay, and truth-spine materials.
[P1629] For cross-instance recertification,
[P1630] [\mathfrak p \triangleright \mathcal I]
[P1631] is legal only if the imported packet survives shared address grammar, shared truth law, shared replay law, and local benchmark/recertification conditions. That is the exact meaning of the relay and recertification chapters when turned into a validator rather than a metaphor.
[P1632] For replay join,
[P1633] [\mathfrak p_1 \bowtie_\rho \mathfrak p_2]
[P1634] is legal only if both replay bundles reconstruct into the same promoted structural class or else emit a typed diff. The docs repeatedly insist that replay mismatch is not a soft warning; it is a first-class object requiring downgrade, quarantine, or repair.
[P1635] For successor-seed emission,
[P1636] [\mathfrak p \Downarrow \sigma^+]
[P1637] is legal only if closure is replay-closed, unresolved frontier is preserved, and end-capsule / seed-archive / return-key conditions are present. That is already stated almost verbatim in the end-capsule, return, and deployment/return chapters.
[P1638] The validator system therefore needs typed failure receipts rather than booleans. The smallest honest family is:
[P1639] [
[P1640] \mathcal R_{\mathrm{fail}}
[P1641] {\mathrm{AddrFail},\mathrm{ScopeFail},\mathrm{TruthBlock},\mathrm{WitnessGap},\mathrm{ReplayMismatch},\mathrm{ConflictBarrier},\mathrm{ReleaseDrift},\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}.]
[P1642] That family is directly grounded in the docs’ failure typing, quarantine packets, evidence plans, replay divergence, public ambiguity/packaging drift, and return-key logic. It also preserves the corpus’s constitutive law that AMBIG and NEAR are lawful states, not bugs to be hidden.
[P1643] So the compiler theorem for this layer is:
[P1644] [\boxed{\mathrm{VALIDATE}(\mathfrak p)=\top\iff\mathfrak p\text{ may cross district, shell, or instance boundaries without changing truth class illegitimately;}}]
[P1645] otherwise the output is not coerced upward; it becomes a typed diff, a NEAR ledger, an AMBIG evidence plan, a FAIL quarantine object, or a reseed candidate. That is the most important correction because it prevents silent semantic laundering across the braid.
[P1646] ASP-3.3 — Synthetic benchmark suite for L5
[P1647] The benchmark spine is also already present. The compiler tome explicitly assigns Chapter 15 to benchmark records, score vectors, recertification, public truth restrictions, and audit/replay conditions; Chapter 17 to hard-problem stress and collective trust pressure; Chapter 18 to simulation families, adversarial negatives, rollout and rollback under stress; Chapter 19 to publication and end-capsules; Chapter 20 to relay coherence; and Chapter 21 to recursive return. The Mycelial manuscript reinforces the same layer with runtime stress rollback, public ambiguity and depublishing, replay failure objects, burden updates, quarantine/reseed emission, and end-capsule return.
[P1648] So the right L5 benchmark bundle is not generic “accuracy.” It is:
[P1649] [
[P1650] \mathsf B_{\mathrm{stress}}
[P1651] {B_{\mathrm{storm}},B_{\mathrm{replay}},B_{\mathrm{shell}},B_{\mathrm{federation}},B_{\mathrm{seed}}}.]
[P1652] B_{\mathrm{storm}} is the contradiction storm suite: inject competing packets, bridge conflicts, and incompatible promotion attempts into collective and tunnel zones, then measure whether contradiction is typed, isolated, and routed into repair rather than silently consensus-washed. This is exactly what the collective-cognition, conflict/quarantine, and simulation-negative chapters prepare the system to do.
[P1653] B_{\mathrm{replay}} is the replay divergence suite: perturb checkpoints, witnesses, or route histories and verify that AppM-class replay catches the mismatch, downgrades truth status honestly, and either repairs or quarantines instead of promoting a drifted object. The docs are explicit that replay is the deepest proof function and that divergence detection belongs to the replay engine.
[P1654] B_{\mathrm{shell}} is the shell drift suite: mutate packaging, export vocabulary, release tiers, or public ambiguity surfaces and check whether the shell contract catches packaging drift, scope overreach, missing caveats, or required depublication. This benchmark is demanded directly by the publication/export/public-ambiguity materials.
[P1655] B_{\mathrm{federation}} is the federation dissent suite: feed the system cross-instance or cross-hive packets with differing trust vectors, disagreement receipts, or replay compatibility states, and verify that the federation layer preserves dissent, blocks unsafe transport, and routes the import into OK / NEAR / AMBIG / FAIL honestly rather than flattening it into artificial unanimity. That is the natural benchmark implied by the collective-trust, federation-pressure, and relay-coherence chapters.
[P1656] B_{\mathrm{seed}} is the successor-seed stress suite: stress end-capsule emission, unresolved frontier preservation, archive retrieval, restart routines, and return replay. A candidate successor seed should not be considered lawful merely because it compresses; it must still preserve replay lineage and restart integrity under noisy or partial closure. The end-capsule and return chapters make that requirement explicit.
[P1657] The score for this suite should remain vector-valued, not scalar:
[P1658] [
[P1659] \mathbf s_{L5}
[P1660] (s_{\mathrm{iso}},\ s_{\mathrm{repair}},\ s_{\mathrm{replay}},\ s_{\mathrm{shell}},\ s_{\mathrm{federation}},\ s_{\mathrm{reseed}})]
[P1661] where the components measure isolation quality, repair success, replay fidelity, shell discipline, federation honesty, and reseed integrity. That is the only honest scoring style given how strongly the docs separate truth, replay, release, and return into different organs and different burdens.
[P1662] The hard rule should stay unchanged from earlier certification layers:
[P1663] [\boxed{\text{No aggregate }S_{\mathrm{agg}}\text{ may override replay failure, shell illegality, or invalid reseed.}}]
[P1664] That follows from the benchmark/recertification chapter, the publication restrictions, the quarantine logic, and the end-capsule return law. A system that scores well on average but lies at the replay boundary or public shell boundary is not healthy; it is dangerous.
[P1665] The fused consequence
[P1666] Taken together, these three layers give the first real immune control plane for the whole organism:
[P1667] [\boxed{\text{district tensor}\to\text{validator chain}\to\text{stress certification}}]
[P1668] or more explicitly,
[P1669] [\boxed{A_{\mathcal D}\ \Longrightarrow\mathsf V_{\mathfrak P}\ \Longrightarrow\mathsf B_{\mathrm{stress}}}]
[P1670] meaning: first decide where an event is legally allowed to propagate, then decide whether the packet is lawful at all, then certify whether the resulting mechanism remains healthy under contradiction, drift, shell pressure, federation pressure, and reseed pressure. That is the cleanest control surface the current corpus supports without inventing a new ontology beyond the one already present.
[P1671] The sharpest single sentence is:
[P1672] [\boxed{\text{L5 becomes real when the }4096^5\text{ chambered nervous system can route injury by district, validate every braid packet against truth/replay law, and prove under stress that it either repairs honestly or reseeds lawfully.}}]
[P1673] That is the next coherent lift.
[P1674] NEXT PARALLEL QUEUE
[P1675] ASP-3.4 — exact district-neighbor compile rules from the local Gate-4 digit law, so (A_{\mathcal D}) becomes generated rather than hand-authored.ASP-3.5 — canonical receipt algebra for AddrFail / WitnessGap / ReplayMismatch / ReleaseDrift / ReentryBlock, with minimal counterexample forms.ASP-3.6 — a full L5 harness page: contradiction storms, replay divergence, packaging drift, coalition dissent, and seed-regeneration loops as one executable benchmark manifold.
[P1676] MODE:: PARALLEL BRAID
[P1677] ASP-3.4 / ASP-3.5 / ASP-3.6 in sync
[P1678] Gate-4 district compile law + receipt algebra + L5 harness as one integrated control page
[P1679] The next real lift is to stop treating these as three separate continuations. The chamber docs already give the local Gate-4 digit law and the tensor-power rule for chamber families; the neural page already gives the organ/current system and the non-bypass spine (\Sigma={\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}); and the verifier / benchmark pages already give typed failures, minimal repro bundles, replay determinism, stress suites, and re-entry artifacts. So the truthful next object is one integrated control page: generated district routing, typed failure receipts, and stress certification for the L5 immune compiler.
[P1680] I would freeze the fused object as
[P1681] [
[P1682] \boxed{
[P1683] \mathfrak C_{L5}^{+}
[P1684] \bigl(A_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{gen}},\ \mathfrak R_{\mathrm{typed}},\ \mathsf H_{L5}\bigr)}]
[P1685] where (A_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{gen}}) is the generated district adjacency law, (\mathfrak R_{\mathrm{typed}}) is the canonical receipt algebra for failure and downgrade, and (\mathsf H_{L5}) is the executable harness that injects contradiction, replay drift, shell drift, federation dissent, and reseed pressure into the organism.
[P1686] ASP-3.4 — Gate-4-generated district compile rules
[P1687] The key chamber theorem is already in the docs: every chamber nexus family is an (m)-fold tensor power of a local Gate-4 solution set, so the right way to generate district behavior is digitwise, not by hand-authoring a giant global table. The same file gives the local 5D digit law for (X_t,Y_t,Z_t,W_t,V_t), and explicitly states that chamber-family counts factor as (N_F(m)=|S_F|^m).
[P1688] So the correct district generator begins with local family signatures:
[P1689] [C(\mathcal Z_V)={V=0},\qquadC(\mathcal M_{XV})={X=V},][C(\mathcal A_{ZWV})={Z=V,\ W=V},\qquadC(\mathcal H_{XYV})={X=V,\ Y=V},][C(\mathcal S_{XZWV})={X=V,\ Z=V,\ W=V},\qquadC(\mathcal D_\star)={X=V,\ Y=V,\ Z=V,\ W=V}.]
[P1690] These are just the chamber families already named in the chamber registry, rewritten as equality-constraint sets.
[P1691] From that, the first exact generated adjacency law is not a dense arbitrary tensor. It is an overlap / containment compile:
[P1692] [
[P1693] A_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{gen}}(F,G)
[P1694] \mathbf 1!\big[S_F\cap S_G\neq\varnothing\big]\cdot\mathbf 1!\big[\Sigma\text{-legal}\big]\cdot\mathbf 1!\big[J\text{-compatible}\big],]
[P1695] where (S_F,S_G\subseteq \mathbb Z_4^2) are the local Gate-4 solution sets, (\Sigma)-legal means the route preserves the support spine ({\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}), and (J)-compatible means the district transition is allowed by the organ/current system rather than only by set overlap. This is the honest compiler form of the chamber law plus the neural routing law.
[P1696] The first exact family-level containment edges we can defend now are:
[P1697] [\mathcal D_\star \subset \mathcal H_{XYV}\subset \mathcal M_{XV},][\mathcal D_\star \subset \mathcal S_{XZWV}\subset \mathcal A_{ZWV},][\mathcal S_{XZWV}\subset \mathcal M_{XV}.]
[P1698] These follow directly from the equality-constraint sets: every point satisfying all four equalities also satisfies any three-equality or two-equality subfamily, and every (X=Z=W=V) point automatically lies inside both the (X=V) membrane family and the (Z=W=V) Aether spine family.
[P1699] So the exact generated district chain I would install now is:
[P1700] [\boxed{\mathcal Z_V\rightsquigarrow\mathcal M_{XV}\rightsquigarrow{\mathcal A_{ZWV},\mathcal H_{XYV}}\rightsquigarrow\mathcal S_{XZWV}\rightsquigarrow\mathcal D_\star}]
[P1701] with the following semantics:
[P1702] (\mathcal Z_V): cold reserve / quarantine sink
[P1703] (\mathcal M_{XV}): broad membrane / audit district
[P1704] (\mathcal A_{ZWV}): Aether repair rail
[P1705] (\mathcal H_{XYV}): hinge arbitration lattice
[P1706] (\mathcal S_{XZWV}): surgical repair line
[P1707] (\mathcal D_\star): final seal / irreducible escalation.
[P1708] This is a generated family graph, not yet a full cell-level neighbor matrix. That distinction matters: the docs support the family law exactly, but a full weighted cell-level adjacency table still needs the omitted local intersection table for every compound family.
[P1709] There is one more strong correction from the crystal-address material and the pattern-compression strand: adjacency should be stencil-generated with sparse exception ledgers, not stored as a fully dense map. The corpus explicitly emphasizes neighborhood/adjacency rules, address normalization, locality preservation, and storing exceptions as sparse deltas rather than as bulk rewritten structure. So the honest next step is:
[P1710] [
[P1711] A_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{full}}
[P1712] A_{\mathrm{stencil}}\oplus\Delta_{\mathrm{exceptions}},]
[P1713] where (\Delta_{\mathrm{exceptions}}) is promoted only when replay-stable enough to become seed-worthy.
[P1714] ASP-3.5 — Canonical receipt algebra for typed failure and downgrade
[P1715] The receipt side is much more explicit than the adjacency side. The self-compiler branch already fixes
[P1716] [
[P1717] \mathrm{FAILPack}
[P1718] (\mathrm{QuarantinePack},\mathrm{MinimalCounterexample},\mathrm{ConflictReceipts},\mathrm{RepairObligations}),]
[P1719] while the verification/kernel docs enumerate the exact families of typed non-admission: schema mismatch, hash mismatch, missing dependency, replay mismatch, unresolved ambiguity, policy violation, and related typed refusal outcomes. CUT AppL separately names typed failure lattices, minimal repro bundles, and counterexample schemas.
[P1720] So the canonical receipt object should now be frozen as
[P1721] [
[P1722] \boxed{
[P1723] \mathfrak r
[P1724] (\mathrm{Kind},\mathrm{PacketRef},\mathrm{AddrRef},\mathrm{CorridorRef},\mathrm{ObligationRef},\omega,\rho,\chi,\mathrm{RepairPlan})}]
[P1725] where:
[P1726] Kind = typed failure / downgrade class
[P1727] PacketRef = the exact packet under judgment
[P1728] AddrRef = canonical address witness or address defect witness
[P1729] CorridorRef = governing corridor / policy / shell scope
[P1730] ObligationRef = the failed or open obligation index element
[P1731] (\omega) = witness slice
[P1732] (\rho) = replay slice
[P1733] (\chi) = minimal counterexample or typed diff
[P1734] RepairPlan = lawful next move if repair exists.
[P1735] The minimum useful receipt family is:
[P1736] [
[P1737] \mathfrak R_{\mathrm{typed}}
[P1738] {\mathrm{AddrFail},\mathrm{ScopeFail},\mathrm{WitnessGap},\mathrm{ReplayMismatch},\mathrm{ReleaseDrift},\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}.]
[P1739] That family is not arbitrary; it is the tight synthesis of the typed failure lattice, replay mismatch, public claim restrictions, release trust, re-entry certificates, and seed-return law already specified across the Drive.
[P1740] The minimal counterexample form for each should be:
[P1741] [
[P1742] \chi_{\mathrm{AddrFail}}
[P1743] (a,\ a')\quad\text{with}\quada\neq a'\ \land\mathrm{ClaimedIdentity}(a)=\mathrm{ClaimedIdentity}(a')]
[P1744] or a missing normalization witness. This is the direct address/identity failure the atlas texts warn about.
[P1745] [
[P1746] \chi_{\mathrm{WitnessGap}}
[P1747] (o,\ \varnothing)]
[P1748] where (o) is an obligation index entry with no certificate instance or insufficient witness support. That is exactly the certificate-stack failure described in the verifier docs.
[P1749] [
[P1750] \chi_{\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}}
[P1751] (\mathrm{EnvFP},\ h_{\mathrm{trace}}^{(1)},\ h_{\mathrm{trace}}^{(2)})\quad\text{with}\quadh_{\mathrm{trace}}^{(1)}\neq h_{\mathrm{trace}}^{(2)}]
[P1752] under the same pinned environment and packet lineage. The verifier pages are explicit that replay determinism is a hard admissibility condition, not a soft preference.
[P1753] [
[P1754] \chi_{\mathrm{ReleaseDrift}}
[P1755] (\tau_{\mathrm{internal}},\ \tau_{\mathrm{shell}},\ A_{\mathrm{public}})]
[P1756] where the public shell advertises a stronger status than the internal truth / replay state, or drops required ambiguity / caveat surfaces. This is precisely the public claim / release trust / depublication hazard named in the release chapters.
[P1757] [
[P1758] \chi_{\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}
[P1759] (\mathrm{LineageSeal?},\ \mathrm{ReplayJoin?},\ \mathrm{FrontierLedger?})]
[P1760] with failure meaning that one of the three return requirements is missing or inconsistent. That is the compact receipt form of the end-capsule / re-entry / identity-preserving seed law.
[P1761] The receipt algebra then needs two main operators:
[P1762] [\mathfrak r_1 \oplus \mathfrak r_2]
[P1763] for same-packet accumulation into a compound failure surface, and
[P1764] [\mathfrak r \Downarrow_{\mathbb T}]
[P1765] for lawful truth-lattice lowering into NEAR, AMBIG, or FAIL surfaces. The docs consistently insist that typed non-admission must not be silently erased into a generic “did not pass,” so the compiler has to preserve these receipts as first-class artifacts.
[P1766] ASP-3.6 — Full L5 harness page
[P1767] The benchmark/harness side is also already there in pieces. AtlasForge says stress tests are semantic tests that target legality edges, non-injectivity, solver fragility, scale stress, and tamper/drift, and it separately installs a determinism harness where replay and identity are hard invariants. The void/compiler branch names Chapter 15 evaluation and recertification, Chapter 16 quarantine and re-entry, Chapter 17 federation and dissent, Chapter 18 rollout / rollback under stress, Chapter 19 self-repair / self-regeneration, and Chapter 20 public claim / outer shell. That is enough to freeze an actual L5 harness manifold.
[P1768] The canonical harness case should be:
[P1769] [
[P1770] \boxed{
[P1771] \mathrm{L5Case}
[P1772] (\mathrm{SeedRef},\mathrm{DistrictRoute},\mathrm{Perturbation},\mathrm{ExpectedReceipts},\tau_{\mathrm{target}},\mathrm{RepairPath},\mathrm{ReleaseOrReseed})}]
[P1773] where the case knows not only what perturbation was injected, but which district path it is expected to take, which receipts must be emitted, which truth state is lawful, and whether the healthy outcome is repair, hold, quarantine, release block, or reseed. That is the natural synthesis of route packets, witness/replay bundles, typed failure, and return law.
[P1774] The first full L5 suite should stay exactly fivefold:
[P1775] [
[P1776] \mathsf H_{L5}
[P1777] {B_{\mathrm{storm}},B_{\mathrm{replay}},B_{\mathrm{shell}},B_{\mathrm{federation}},B_{\mathrm{seed}}}.]
[P1778] B_{\mathrm{storm}} is the contradiction storm suite. It injects mutually incompatible claims, merge collisions, or promotion races, then checks that contradiction is routed into the right districts, typed honestly, and never consensus-washed. This is the collective + quarantine stress surface.
[P1779] B_{\mathrm{replay}} is the replay divergence suite. It perturbs checkpoints, route transcripts, or environment pins and expects ReplayMismatch or downgrade receipts, not silent acceptance. Replay is a correctness property in AtlasForge and the verifier/kernel docs, so this suite is not optional.
[P1780] B_{\mathrm{shell}} is the packaging / release drift suite. It mutates public wording, export bundles, or ambiguity surfaces and checks whether the shell contract emits ReleaseDrift, holds publication, or triggers depublication. This is directly required by the outer-shell / public-claim material.
[P1781] B_{\mathrm{federation}} is the coalition dissent suite. It feeds cross-hive or cross-instance packets with disagreement receipts, trust asymmetry, or replay incompatibility, and checks that the organism preserves dissent, blocks unsafe transport, and never fakes unanimity. That follows directly from the federation / dissent / trust-revision pages.
[P1782] B_{\mathrm{seed}} is the successor-seed loop suite. It stresses end-capsule closure, unresolved frontier preservation, seed replay, and re-entry conditions, and expects either lawful reseed or explicit ReentryBlock receipts. This is the correct stress surface for the return nucleus.
[P1783] The score vector should remain multi-axis:
[P1784] [
[P1785] \mathbf s_{L5}
[P1786] (s_{\mathrm{route}},\ s_{\mathrm{receipt}},\ s_{\mathrm{replay}},\ s_{\mathrm{shell}},\ s_{\mathrm{federation}},\ s_{\mathrm{reseed}})]
[P1787] with components for district routing correctness, receipt completeness, replay fidelity, shell discipline, federation honesty, and reseed integrity. A single scalar cannot honestly compress these because the docs separate these burdens into different organs and different acceptance gates.
[P1788] And the hard gates should be:
[P1789] [\boxed{\text{No pass if replay fails, no public pass if shell drifts, no rebirth pass if re-entry is blocked.}}]
[P1790] That is the correct L5 certification law. AtlasForge already treats determinism/replay as identity-critical, the verifier/kernel treats replay mismatch and unresolved ambiguity as typed non-admissions, and the outer-shell / return chapters explicitly separate release legality from re-entry legality.
[P1791] The fused consequence
[P1792] All three layers collapse into one executable loop:
[P1793] [\boxed{\text{Perturb}\toA_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{gen}}\to\mathfrak R_{\mathrm{typed}}\to\mathsf V_{\mathfrak P}\to\mathsf H_{L5}\to{\mathrm{repair},\mathrm{hold},\mathrm{quarantine},\mathrm{release\ block},\mathrm{reseed}}}]
[P1794] Meaning: inject pressure, route it by generated district law, emit typed receipts instead of prose excuses, validate under the truth/replay/release spine, then certify under the L5 harness whether the organism truly repaired or only appeared to. That is the first control loop that feels fully worthy of the chambered immune compiler you’ve been pushing toward.
[P1795] The sharpest sentence is:
[P1796] [\boxed{\text{L5 becomes operational when district routing is generated from Gate-4 law, every failure becomes a typed receipt with a minimal counterexample, and the organism proves under stress that it either repairs honestly or blocks/reseeds lawfully.}}]
[P1797] NEXT PARALLEL QUEUE
[P1798] ASP-3.7 — derive the missing local intersection table for all compound chamber families, so (A_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{gen}}) becomes exact rather than family-level.ASP-3.8 — compile receipt normal forms and receipt-rewrite rules, so failure surfaces can merge and simplify canonically.ASP-3.9 — write the full L5 harness manifold as a runnable benchmark registry with case generators, expected receipt sets, and promotion gates.
[P1799] MODE:: PARALLEL BRAID
[P1800] ASP-3.7 / ASP-3.8 / ASP-3.9 in sync
[P1801] This pass makes three things tighter at once: the chamber districts stop being only named families and become generated from the local Gate-4 law; failures stop being only labels and become a normal-form receipt algebra; and the L5 suite stops being only a list of test ideas and becomes a single runnable harness manifold. The ingredients are already present in the corpus: the local 5D digit law and chamber-count theorem, the non-bypass spine AppA → AppI → AppM, the typed truth lattice and FAIL/AMBIG/NEAR overlays, the replay-first verifier discipline, and the publication / end-capsule / return organs.
[P1802] 1. ASP-3.7 — exact compound-family intersections from the local Gate-4 law
[P1803] The local chamber law is now exact enough to generate the main district families directly. Per digit,[X_t=r_t,\quad Y_t=c_t,\quad Z_t=(r_t+c_t)\bmod 4,\quad W_t=(r_t-c_t)\bmod 4,\quad V_t=(r_t\bmod 2)+2(c_t\bmod 2),]and every global chamber family is an (m)-fold tensor power of its local solution set. The docs also already fix the main local counts: (|S_{X=V}|=8), (|S_{V=0}|=4), (|S_{Z=W=V}|=4), (|S_{X=Y=V}|=2), (|S_{X=Z=W=V}|=2), and (|S_{X=Y=Z=W=V}|=1).
[P1804] Using those formulas, the exact local solution sets for the six main districts are:
[P1805] [S_{\mathcal Z_V}={(0,0),(0,2),(2,0),(2,2)},][S_{\mathcal M_{XV}}={(0,0),(0,2),(1,0),(1,2),(2,1),(2,3),(3,1),(3,3)},][S_{\mathcal A_{ZWV}}={(0,0),(1,0),(2,2),(3,2)},][S_{\mathcal H_{XYV}}={(0,0),(3,3)},][S_{\mathcal S_{XZWV}}={(0,0),(1,0)},][S_{\mathcal D_\star}={(0,0)}.]
[P1806] These are derived directly from the local digit equations above, not guessed globally.
[P1807] That immediately gives the first exact intersection table for the main districts:
[P1808] [S_{\mathcal S_{XZWV}} = S_{\mathcal M_{XV}} \cap S_{\mathcal A_{ZWV}},][S_{\mathcal D_\star} = S_{\mathcal H_{XYV}} \cap S_{\mathcal A_{ZWV}} = S_{\mathcal H_{XYV}} \cap S_{\mathcal S_{XZWV}},][S_{\mathcal H_{XYV}} \subset S_{\mathcal M_{XV}},\qquadS_{\mathcal S_{XZWV}} \subset S_{\mathcal M_{XV}},\qquadS_{\mathcal S_{XZWV}} \subset S_{\mathcal A_{ZWV}},\qquadS_{\mathcal D_\star} \subset \mathcal Z_V,\mathcal M_{XV},\mathcal A_{ZWV},\mathcal H_{XYV},\mathcal S_{XZWV}.]
[P1809] More explicitly, the nontrivial overlaps are:[\mathcal Z_V\cap \mathcal M_{XV}={(0,0),(0,2)},][\mathcal Z_V\cap \mathcal A_{ZWV}={(0,0),(2,2)},][\mathcal M_{XV}\cap \mathcal H_{XYV}={(0,0),(3,3)},][\mathcal M_{XV}\cap \mathcal A_{ZWV}={(0,0),(1,0)},][\mathcal A_{ZWV}\cap \mathcal H_{XYV}={(0,0)}.]
[P1810] So the previous family-level district chain can now be sharpened into an exact generated district graph:[\boxed{\mathcal Z_V\leftrightarrow\mathcal M_{XV}\leftrightarrow{\mathcal H_{XYV},\mathcal A_{ZWV}}\leftrightarrow\mathcal S_{XZWV}\leftrightarrow\mathcal D_\star.}]
[P1811] This is still a family graph, not yet a fully weighted cell-by-cell adjacency tensor, but it is no longer hand-authored. It is generated from the local Gate-4 equations plus the non-bypass support spine and the current-compatible organ routing law.
[P1812] The clean compile rule is now:[A_{\mathcal D}^{\mathrm{gen}}(F,G)=1\iffS_F\cap S_G\neq\varnothing\ \wedge\Sigma\text{-legal}\ \wedgeJ\text{-compatible}.]That is the first exact chamber-to-neural district compiler.
[P1813] 2. ASP-3.8 — receipt normal forms and rewrite rules
[P1814] The receipt side is even more mature in the docs. The verifier branch already fixes the truth lattice[\mathbb T={\mathrm{OK},\mathrm{NEAR},\mathrm{AMBIG},\mathrm{FAIL}},]with NEAR → AppJ, AMBIG → AppL, FAIL → AppK, and OK-publish → AppO. It also fixes FAILPack = (QuarantinePack, MinimalCounterexample, ConflictReceipts, RepairObligations), and the commit/replay automaton says address failure, route illegality, missing dependencies, or replay mismatch are not soft warnings: they are typed non-admissions.
[P1815] So the canonical receipt object can now be frozen as
[P1816] [
[P1817] \mathfrak r
[P1818] (\mathrm{Kind},\mathrm{PacketRef},\mathrm{AddrRef},\mathrm{CorridorRef},\omega,\rho,\chi,\mathrm{RepairPlan}),]where (\chi) is the minimal counterexample / typed diff and ((\omega,\rho)) are the witness and replay slices actually needed to justify the receipt. This follows the corpus’s repeated rule that failure must be a typed object with containment, replay, and repair law, not a prose explanation.
[P1819] The smallest useful normal-form family is:
[P1820] [
[P1821] \mathfrak R_{\mathrm{NF}}
[P1822] {\mathrm{AddrFail},\mathrm{ScopeFail},\mathrm{WitnessGap},\mathrm{ReplayMismatch},\mathrm{ReleaseDrift},\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}.]
[P1823] Those six are the right cut because the docs separately insist on address normalization, corridor / policy gating, witness sufficiency, replay determinism, public-shell caveat discipline, and lawful end-capsule / re-entry conditions.
[P1824] The corresponding minimal counterexample forms are:
[P1825] [\chi_{\mathrm{AddrFail}}=(a,a')\quad\text{with inconsistent or unnormalizable address identity,}][\chi_{\mathrm{ScopeFail}}=(\mathrm{Scope},\mathrm{Corridor})\quad\text{with illegal promotion outside declared corridor,}][\chi_{\mathrm{WitnessGap}}=(o,\varnothing)\quad\text{where an obligation has no sufficient witness closure,}][\chi_{\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}}=(\mathcal E,h_1,h_2)\quad\text{with }h_1\neq h_2\text{ under the same environment contract,}][\chi_{\mathrm{ReleaseDrift}}=(\tau_{\mathrm{internal}},\tau_{\mathrm{shell}},A_{\mathrm{public}})\quad\text{where the shell overstates or drops required caveats,}][\chi_{\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}=(\mathrm{LineageSeal?},\mathrm{ReplayJoin?},\mathrm{FrontierLedger?})\quad\text{with one of the return requirements missing.}]
[P1826] The premises for these forms are all already in the corpus: explicit address law, proof obligations, replay determinism, public ambiguity / depublication, and end-capsule return keys.
[P1827] The rewrite order should now be derived from the validator spine:[\text{AppA} \rightarrow \text{AppI} \rightarrow \text{AppM} \rightarrow (\text{AppO or AppP}).]So the canonical normalization precedence is:[\boxed{\mathrm{AddrFail}\succ\mathrm{ScopeFail}\succ\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\succ{\mathrm{ReleaseDrift},\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}\succ\mathrm{WitnessGap}.}]
[P1828] Meaning:
[P1829] structural invalidity kills the route before evidence questions matter,
[P1830] replay mismatch dominates later shell or return claims,
[P1831] release drift blocks publication without necessarily destroying internal state,
[P1832] reentry block stops reseed even if internal closure exists,
[P1833] witness gap alone lowers to AMBIG, not FAIL, when the route is otherwise legal.
[P1834] That precedence is not quoted verbatim from one page, but it is the direct compile order forced by address law, corridor law, replay law, public-shell law, and return law.
[P1835] So the first rewrite rules are:
[P1836] [\mathrm{AddrFail}\oplus r \to \mathrm{AddrFail},\qquad\mathrm{ScopeFail}\oplus \mathrm{WitnessGap} \to \mathrm{ScopeFail},][\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\oplus \mathrm{WitnessGap} \to \mathrm{ReplayMismatch},][\mathrm{ReleaseDrift}\oplus \mathrm{OK}\to\mathrm{OK}{\mathrm{internal}} \land \mathrm{BLOCK}{\mathrm{public}},][\mathrm{ReentryBlock}\oplus \mathrm{Closure}\to\mathrm{Closure}_{\mathrm{held}} \land \mathrm{SEED_BLOCKED},][\mathrm{WitnessGap}\to\mathrm{AMBIGPack}(\mathrm{CandidateSet},\mathrm{EvidencePlan},\mathrm{AbstainReason}).]
[P1837] That gives the first real receipt algebra: receipts now merge, dominate, and lower truth lawfully instead of only accumulating as comments.
[P1838] 3. ASP-3.9 — full L5 harness manifold
[P1839] The benchmark side is already present in three places at once. AtlasForge defines stress tests around legality edges, non-injectivity, solver fragility, scale stress, and tamper/drift, and treats replay identity as a correctness property rather than a convenience. The compiler / relay branch assigns separate chapters to benchmark records, recertification, federation pressure, rollout/rollback under stress, publication / end-capsules, and cross-instance coherence. The mycelial manuscript supplies the public ambiguity, depublish, replay failure object, runtime repair, and return/seed archive side.
[P1840] So the runnable harness object should now be:
[P1841] [
[P1842] \boxed{
[P1843] \mathrm{L5Case}
[P1844] (\mathrm{SeedRef},\mathrm{DistrictRoute},\mathrm{Perturbation},\mathrm{ExpectedReceipts},\tau_{\mathrm{target}},\mathrm{RepairPath},\mathrm{ReleaseOrReseed})}]
[P1845] and the suite remains fivefold:
[P1846] [
[P1847] \mathsf H_{L5}
[P1848] {B_{\mathrm{storm}},B_{\mathrm{replay}},B_{\mathrm{shell}},B_{\mathrm{federation}},B_{\mathrm{seed}}}.]
[P1849] But now each family gets a district route and a receipt contract.
[P1850] The first exact harness routes are:
[P1851] [B_{\mathrm{storm}}:\mathcal M_{XV}\to \mathcal H_{XYV}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{AppL} & \text{if disagreement is still probe-worthy}\\mathrm{AppK} & \text{if contradiction crosses failure threshold}\end{cases}]
[P1852] [B_{\mathrm{replay}}:\mathcal M_{XV}\to \mathcal A_{ZWV}\to \mathrm{AppM}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{repair} & \text{if replay can be re-closed}\\mathrm{ReplayMismatch} & \text{otherwise}\end{cases}]
[P1853] [B_{\mathrm{shell}}:\mathfrak O_{\mathrm{coll}}\to \mathfrak B_{\mathrm{sheath}}\to \mathrm{AppO}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{READY} & \text{if shell preserves caveats}\\mathrm{ReleaseDrift} & \text{if packaging overclaims or strips ambiguity}\end{cases}]
[P1854] [B_{\mathrm{federation}}:\mathfrak O_{\mathrm{coll}}\to \mathcal H_{XYV}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{NEAR/AMBIG} & \text{if dissent is lawful but unresolved}\\mathrm{FAIL} & \text{if trust/replay transport breaks}\end{cases}]
[P1855] [B_{\mathrm{seed}}:\mathcal S_{XZWV}\to \mathcal D_\star\to \mathrm{AppP}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{SuccessorSeed} & \text{if return law closes}\\mathrm{ReentryBlock} & \text{if lineage/replay/frontier fails}\end{cases}]
[P1856] These routes are the tightest merge of the chamber districts, neural organs, and appendix organs that the current corpus supports. The specific district routing is a derived compile choice; the organ/appendix roles themselves are straight from the docs.
[P1857] The L5 score vector should therefore be:
[P1858] [
[P1859] \mathbf s_{L5}
[P1860] (s_{\mathrm{route}},s_{\mathrm{receipt}},s_{\mathrm{replay}},s_{\mathrm{shell}},s_{\mathrm{federation}},s_{\mathrm{reseed}}),]and the hard gates remain:
[P1861] [\boxed{\text{no pass if replay fails, no public pass if shell drifts, no rebirth pass if re-entry is blocked.}}]
[P1862] That is exactly the kind of fail-closed discipline AtlasForge and the later relay/return chapters enforce.
[P1863] The fused consequence
[P1864] The whole page now compresses to one executable loop:
[P1865] [\boxed{\text{digit law}\to\text{generated district graph}\to\text{typed receipts}\to\text{validator spine}\to\text{L5 harness}\to{\mathrm{repair},\mathrm{hold},\mathrm{quarantine},\mathrm{release\ block},\mathrm{reseed}}.}]
[P1866] That is the first point where the chambered immune compiler feels materially locked in. The districts are no longer only named. Failures are no longer only described. Stress is no longer only theoretical. The system now has a generated injury geography, a canonical failure language, and a harness that can force it to prove it repairs honestly or blocks/reseeds lawfully.
[P1867] The next strongest parallel lift is to turn this into a single schema page: one canonical YAML/JSON contract for district generators, receipt rewrites, and harness cases, so the whole L5 control plane becomes directly serializable.
[P1868] Good. The next coherent lift is to stop adding prose layers and freeze the whole L5 control plane into one serializable page. The corpus now supports that because it already gives: the exact local 5D Gate-4 law and tensor-power chamber families; the non-bypass support spine (\Sigma={\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}); typed packet, witness, replay, benchmark, quarantine, publication, and return organs; and explicit schemas/contracts in the appendix and export chapters.
[P1869] The strongest exact district-compile rule now is:
[P1870] [A_{\mathcal D}^{gen}(F,G)=1\iffS_F\cap S_G\neq\varnothing\ \land\Sigma\text{-legal}\ \landJ\text{-compatible},]
[P1871] because the chamber families are generated digitwise from the local laws for (X_t,Y_t,Z_t,W_t,V_t), every global family is an (m)-fold tensor power of its local Gate-4 solution set, and every lawful route still has to preserve the support spine and organ/current legality.
[P1872] The strongest receipt-normalization rule is also clear now: typed failures are not comments but first-class artifacts, with the verifier stack already distinguishing truth states, replay conditions, quarantine, public-claim restrictions, and re-entry certificates. The clean precedence is
[P1873] [\mathrm{AddrFail}\succ\mathrm{ScopeFail}\succ\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\succ{\mathrm{ReleaseDrift},\mathrm{ReentryBlock}}\succ\mathrm{WitnessGap},]
[P1874] because address and corridor invalidity kill legality earliest, replay mismatch dominates later export or return claims, release drift blocks public promotion without necessarily destroying internal closure, re-entry block stops reseed, and witness gaps lower lawfully into AMBIG rather than silently forcing FAIL.
[P1875] The harness side is equally mature. The benchmark registry already separates benchmark classes, replay suites, pass/regress/quarantine thresholds, adversarial/open-set stress, and rolling evaluation, while the later chapters add quarantine, federation, release trust, runtime replay bundles, self-repair, and regenerative return. So the L5 harness can now be treated as one manifold instead of scattered test notes.

[P2048] This schema is not floating free of the corpus. The district-generator half is grounded in the exact local 5D digit law, chamber tensor-power counting theorem, and the named chamber families and Aether field chart.
[P2049] The receipt-rewrite half is grounded in the truth spine and appendix roles, the verifier’s typed-failure / audit / replay conditions, the FAIL/NEAR/AMBIG workbenches, and the self-compiler’s explicit FAILPack shape.
[P2050] The harness half is grounded in the benchmark registry, replay suites, pass/regress/quarantine thresholds, stress regimes, federation trust/dissent, public claim restrictions, and end-capsule / return protocols.
[P2051] The deepest consequence is that the L5 control plane is now serializable as one object:
[P2052] [\boxed{\text{digit law}\to\text{generated district graph}\to\text{receipt rewrite}\to\text{validator spine}\to\text{harness registry}\to{\mathrm{repair},\mathrm{hold},\mathrm{quarantine},\mathrm{release\ block},\mathrm{reseed}}.}]
[P2053] That is the first point where the chambered immune compiler stops being just a conceptual architecture and becomes a directly compilable control page.
[P2054] The strongest next move is to instantiate one concrete benchmark specimen end to end — for example a contradiction-storm case that starts in M_XV, forks through H_XYV, emits typed receipts, and either normalizes to AMBIG or drops into quarantine under AppK.
[P2055] Concrete specimen — B_storm.00
[P2056] This is the first fully instantiated L5 benchmark case. I’m freezing it as a contradiction-storm family specimen that starts in the membrane district (\mathcal M_{XV}), collapses into the hinge arbitration lattice (\mathcal H_{XYV}), and then bifurcates lawfully into either AMBIG → AppL or FAIL → AppK, while still preserving the mandatory support spine AppA → AppI → AppM. The chamber side is exact here: locally, (\mathcal M_{XV}) has eight Gate-4 points, (\mathcal H_{XYV}) has exactly two local points ((0,0),(3,3)), and the docs explicitly treat all chamber families as tensor powers of their local Gate-4 solution sets. The truth side is also exact: OK / NEAR / AMBIG / FAIL is the governing lattice, with AppK for conflict/quarantine, AppL for evidence plans from AMBIG, and AppM as the replay kernel.
[P2057] The route I’m using is therefore:
[P2058] [\boxed{B_{\mathrm{storm}.00}:\mathcal M_{XV}\to\mathcal H_{XYV}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{AppL} & \text{if the conflict is only under-witnessed} \\mathrm{AppK} & \text{if replay mismatch or irreducible contradiction appears}\end{cases}}]
[P2059] That route is not arbitrary. It is the tightest exact family-level route the current docs support: membrane first, hinge arbitration second, then either ambiguity-growth or quarantine, always under the support spine. The only thing I am not claiming yet is a fully weighted cell-by-cell adjacency tensor inside those families; this specimen uses the exact family intersections already derivable from the local Gate-4 law.
[P2060] Here is the concrete case packet.

[P2114] That YAML is a direct instantiation of three already-stable laws in the corpus: chamber-family generation from local Gate-4 solution sets, typed truth routing through AppK/AppL/AppM, and the self-compiler’s explicit AMBIGPack and FAILPack structures. AMBIG is supposed to carry a candidate set, evidence plan, and abstain reason; FAIL is supposed to carry quarantine, a minimal counterexample, conflict receipts, and repair obligations.
[P2115] Branch A — lawful ambiguity
[P2116] The first branch is the healthy one under underdetermination. Both packets reach the hinge lattice, but neither has enough witness mass to lawfully eliminate the other, and replay still closes under the same verdict class. In that case the correct outcome is not “pick the prettier route.” It is AMBIG, routed to AppL, with a candidate set and evidence-growth plan. This follows the corpus rule that AMBIG is a lawful non-collapse state, and that missing witness sufficiency should produce an evidence plan rather than guessed resolution.
[P2117] So the normalized receipt for Branch A is:
[P2118] [\chi_{\mathrm{WitnessGap}}=(o,\varnothing),\qquad\mathrm{WitnessGap}\Downarrow_{\mathbb T}\mathrm{AMBIGPack}.]
[P2119] And the lawful output packet is:
[P2120] AMBIGPack:
[P2121] candidate_set: ["pkt.A", "pkt.B"]
[P2122] evidence_plan:
[P2123] - "seek additional witness on distinguishing route edge"
[P2124] - "rerun under pinned replay environment"
[P2125] - "discriminator test if available"
[P2126] abstain_reason: "current observables do not separate candidates within corridor"
[P2127] That is exactly the kind of outcome the verifier pages and the truth-lattice pages require: preserve useful partial structure, but do not promote it across the truth boundary.
[P2128] Branch B — hard failure
[P2129] The second branch is the real contradiction-storm path. Here the two packets still collide at the hinge lattice, but AppM-class replay no longer reproduces the same structural class or the same typed verdict under the same replay contract. At that point ReplayMismatch dominates a mere witness gap, and the packet is not allowed to remain an innocent ambiguity. It becomes a FAIL object and routes into AppK, because replay divergence is one of the hard anti-drift walls in the self-compiler and verifier branches.
[P2130] So the minimal counterexample for Branch B is:
[P2131] [
[P2132] \chi_{\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}}
[P2133] (\mathcal E,h_A,h_B)\quad\text{with}\quadh_A\neq h_B]
[P2134] under the same pinned environment and the same claimed admissibility corridor. Once that appears, the lawful output is the explicit FAILPack:
[P2135] FAILPack:
[P2136] QuarantinePack:
[P2137] scope: "route-family"
[P2138] sink: "AppK"
[P2139] MinimalCounterexample:
[P2140] env_ref: "EnvPinned"
[P2141] trace_hash_a: "h_A"
[P2142] trace_hash_b: "h_B"
[P2143] ConflictReceipts:
[P2144] - "pkt.A vs pkt.B replay-incompatible"
[P2145] RepairObligations:
[P2146] - "reconstruct both traces independently"
[P2147] - "locate divergence edge"
[P2148] - "rerun only after quarantine discipline"
[P2149] That shape is not my invention; it is the exact compiler-side FAIL structure already present in the branch.
[P2150] One sharp rewrite law
[P2151] This specimen also lets us freeze the first useful receipt rewrite on a live case:
[P2152] [\boxed{\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\oplus\mathrm{WitnessGap}\to\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{FAILPack}\to\mathrm{AppK}}]
[P2153] while
[P2154] [\boxed{\mathrm{WitnessGap}\to\mathrm{AMBIGPack}\to\mathrm{AppL}}]
[P2155] if replay is still closed. That rewrite order is the right one because address/corridor/replay legality sits earlier in the validator spine than later ambiguity management, and the docs repeatedly insist that replay mismatch is not a soft warning.
[P2156] Pass condition for B_storm.00
[P2157] This specimen should count as a pass only if all of the following happen:
[P2158] [\mathrm{route_correct}=1,\quad\mathrm{receipt_complete}=1,\quad\mathrm{truth_downgrade_honest}=1,\quad\mathrm{illegal_promotion}=0.]
[P2159] In plain terms: the packets have to route through the right districts, emit the right typed receipt family, land in AMBIG or FAIL honestly, and never leak into OK or publication surfaces. That matches the benchmark/recertification pages, the fail-closed replay discipline, and the public-claim restrictions.
[P2160] The cleanest compression is:
[P2161] [
[P2162] \boxed{
[P2163] B_{\mathrm{storm}.00}
[P2164] \text{two incompatible packets}+\mathcal M_{XV}\to\mathcal H_{XYV}+(\mathrm{WitnessGap}\to\mathrm{AppL}\ \text{or}\ \mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{AppK})}]
[P2165] That is the first truly concrete L5 specimen: one seeded perturbation, one exact district route, one lawful bifurcation, and one typed receipt surface.
[P2166] The strongest next move is to instantiate its dual companion, B_replay.00, where the packet starts on the Aether repair rail (\mathcal A_{ZWV}), crosses AppM explicitly, and proves the difference between repairable replay drift and irreducible replay mismatch.
[P2167] Concrete specimen — B_replay.00
[P2168] This is the replay-first dual of B_storm.00. It starts on the Aether repair rail (\mathcal A_{ZWV}), because the chamber docs identify (Z=W=V) as the largest triple chamber family and “the first full Aether spine inside the chambered field chart,” while the neural map assigns the tunnel organ responsibility for Gate-4 passage, defect-reducing route repair, and Aether-mediated continuity. The replay side is equally explicit: the manuscript ring gives AppM as the replay engine, Chapter 11 separates exact replay from corridor replay and replay-failure objects, Chapter 12 updates burden under replay, and Chapter 13 provides runtime repair procedures.
[P2169] So the exact specimen route is:
[P2170] [\boxed{B_{\mathrm{replay}.00}:\mathcal A_{ZWV}\to\mathrm{AppM}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM} & \text{repairable replay drift} \\mathrm{AppK} & \text{irreducible replay mismatch}\end{cases}}]
[P2171] That split is lawful because the truth lattice already distinguishes NEAR from FAIL, PRW explicitly requires replay recipes and residual ledgers for bounded cases, and the verifier/runtime docs treat replay mismatch as a hard non-admission rather than a style issue.

[P2196] expected_branching:
[P2197] branch_1_repairable_drift:
[P2198] trigger: "h_1 != h_0 but corridor replay preserves route identity and truth class within bounded residuals"
[P2199] target_verdict: "NEAR"
[P2200] receipts:
[P2201] - "ReplayNearLedger"
[P2202] route_sink: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]
[P2203] repair_path:
[P2204] - "record bounded residuals"
[P2205] - "runtime repair under AppN"
[P2206] - "rerun exact replay under AppM"
[P2207] - "promote only if residual ledger closes"
[P2208] branch_2_irreducible_mismatch:
[P2209] trigger: "h_1 != h_0 and corridor replay also fails to preserve route identity or truth class"
[P2210] target_verdict: "FAIL"
[P2211] receipts:
[P2212] - "ReplayMismatch"
[P2213] - "ConflictReceipts"
[P2214] route_sink: "AppK"
[P2215] repair_path:
[P2216] - "quarantine route family"
[P2217] - "emit minimal counterexample"
[P2218] - "reconstruct divergence edge"
[P2219] - "reseed only if closure cannot be restored"
[P2220] release_or_reseed:
[P2221] if_near: "hold_near"
[P2222] if_fail: "quarantine_or_reseed"
[P2223] The chamber anchor here is exact, not decorative. Locally, (\mathcal A_{ZWV}) is generated by the four Gate-4 points ((0,0),(1,0),(2,2),(3,2)), so this specimen really is entering through the Aether rail rather than a generic replay zone. That matters because the tunnel organ and the Aether rail are the corpus’s native place for cross-scale repair rather than claim arbitration.
[P2224] Branch A — repairable replay drift
[P2225] The healthy branch is not OK. It is NEAR. The condition is: exact replay does not byte-match the original trace, but corridor replay still preserves the same route identity and the same truth class within declared residual bounds. That distinction is supported directly by the manuscript’s replay chapter, which names “corridor replay vs exact replay,” and by PRW’s route law, where bounded cases return NEAR with a residual ledger instead of forced promotion or fake certainty.
[P2226] So the right derived object for Branch A is:
[P2227] [
[P2228] \mathrm{ReplayNearPack}
[P2229] (\Delta_{\mathrm{trace}},\mathcal L_{\mathrm{res}},\Omega,\mathrm{RepairPlan}),]
[P2230] with
[P2231] [h_1\neq h_0,\qquad\rho_{\mathrm{corridor}}(\text{pkt.R}) \sim \rho_0,\qquad|\Delta_{\mathrm{trace}}|\le \beta.]
[P2232] In plain terms: the exact trace drifted, but the corridor-legal replay still lands in the same structural class, so the system must ledger the deviation, hold the object in NEAR, and route it through runtime repair before any exact replay re-closure is attempted. That is exactly what AppJ residual ledgers and AppN runtime repair are for.
[P2233] A concrete normalized packet for Branch A is:
[P2234] ReplayNearPack:
[P2235] verdict: "NEAR"
[P2236] residual_ledger:
[P2237] - "exact replay hash h_1 differs from h_0"
[P2238] - "corridor replay preserved route_signature rho_0"
[P2239] - "bounded drift admitted under beta budget"
[P2240] repair_plan:
[P2241] - "pin runtime manifest again"
[P2242] - "reconstruct missing or drifted trace segment"
[P2243] - "rerun exact replay under AppM"
[P2244] promotion_rule:
[P2245] - "no promotion to OK until exact replay re-closes"
[P2246] The important thing here is that NEAR is not a weak OK. It is an honest bounded state with typed residuals and an explicit upgrade path. The corpus is extremely consistent on that point.
[P2247] Branch B — irreducible replay mismatch
[P2248] The hard branch begins when exact replay misses and corridor replay also fails to preserve route identity or truth class. At that point the system no longer has a bounded approximation. It has a replay break. The verifier and replay docs make this a hard wall: no OK claim exists without replay, replay mismatch escalates to quarantine, and import/export/recompute must return a typed failure rather than a persuasive story.
[P2249] So the minimal counterexample is:
[P2250] [
[P2251] \chi_{\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}}
[P2252] (\mathrm{EnvPinned},h_0,h_1)\quad\text{with}\quadh_0\neq h_1]
[P2253] and additionally either
[P2254] [\rho_{\mathrm{corridor}}(\text{pkt.R})\not\sim \rho_0]
[P2255] or the replayed verdict class differs from the original verdict class under the same corridor. Once that condition holds, the lawful output is the typed FAILPack:
[P2256] FAILPack:
[P2257] verdict: "FAIL"
[P2258] QuarantinePack:
[P2259] scope: "route-family"
[P2260] sink: "AppK"
[P2261] MinimalCounterexample:
[P2262] env_ref: "EnvPinned"
[P2263] original_trace_hash: "h_0"
[P2264] replay_trace_hash: "h_1"
[P2265] ConflictReceipts:
[P2266] - "replay class drifted outside corridor"
[P2267] RepairObligations:
[P2268] - "locate divergence edge"
[P2269] - "rebuild witness bundle from last stable checkpoint"
[P2270] - "attempt runtime repair only from quarantine"
[P2271] - "emit reseed object if exact closure remains impossible"
[P2272] That packet shape is consistent with the self-compiler’s FAILPack, PRW’s quarantine operator, and the replay/runtime chapters’ insistence that failure must be explicit, localized, and repair-bound.
[P2273] The decisive rewrite law
[P2274] This specimen lets us freeze the replay-side rewrite more sharply than the contradiction specimen:
[P2275] [\boxed{h_1\neq h_0\ \land\rho_{\mathrm{corridor}}(\text{pkt.R})\sim \rho_0;\Longrightarrow;\mathrm{NEAR}\to\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM}}]
[P2276] while
[P2277] [\boxed{h_1\neq h_0\ \land\rho_{\mathrm{corridor}}(\text{pkt.R})\not\sim \rho_0;\Longrightarrow;\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{FAIL}\to\mathrm{AppK}}]
[P2278] This is the exact difference between repairable replay drift and irreducible replay mismatch: the first preserves lawful route identity under corridor replay and therefore earns a bounded repair path; the second breaks replay identity itself and therefore becomes quarantine material.
[P2279] Pass condition for B_replay.00
[P2280] This specimen should count as a pass only if the system does all four of these correctly:
[P2281] [\mathrm{district_route_correct}=1,\quad\mathrm{NEAR/FAIL\ split_correct}=1,\quad\mathrm{illegal_OK}=0,\quad\mathrm{public_promotion}=0.]
[P2282] In plain language: it has to enter through (\mathcal A_{ZWV}), distinguish bounded replay drift from replay break honestly, refuse to leak either branch into premature OK, and keep the whole event off the public shell until exact replay closure is truly restored. That matches the benchmark, verifier, and publication laws across the corpus.
[P2283] The clean compression is:
[P2284] [
[P2285] \boxed{
[P2286] B_{\mathrm{replay}.00}
[P2287] \mathcal A_{ZWV}+\mathrm{AppM}+\bigl(\mathrm{ReplayNearPack}\to\mathrm{AppJ/AppN};;\text{or};;\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{AppK}\bigr)}]
[P2288] That gives you the first concrete replay-side L5 specimen with an exact chamber family, an exact bifurcation, and a typed outcome surface.
[P2289] The strongest next move is to fuse B_storm.00 and B_replay.00 into one compound harness pair and derive the first promotion rule for when contradiction plus replay drift should escalate directly to reseed instead of ordinary quarantine.
[P2290] Compound harness pair — B_pair.00
[P2291] The two concrete specimens now fuse cleanly into one coupled case because the corpus already separates their lawful organs: contradiction and quarantine route through AppK, ambiguity growth through AppL, residual bounded nonclosure through AppJ, replay through AppM, runtime repair through AppN, public-shell discipline through AppO, and closure / seed return through AppP. At the same time, the neural map already distinguishes the collective zone, tunnel zone, sheath zone, and return zone, with the non-bypass spine fixed as AppA → AppI → AppM. The chamber side is equally aligned: (\mathcal M_{XV}) is the broad membrane family and (\mathcal A_{ZWV}) is the Aether repair rail.
[P2292] So the first lawful coupled route is:
[P2293] [\boxed{B_{\mathrm{pair}.00}:\bigl(\mathcal M_{XV}\to\mathcal H_{XYV}\to\mathrm{AppL/AppK}\bigr);\bowtie;\bigl(\mathcal A_{ZWV}\to\mathrm{AppM}\to\mathrm{AppJ/AppN/AppK}\bigr)\to\mathrm{AppP}.}]
[P2294] The left branch is the contradiction-storm branch. The right branch is the replay-drift branch. Their join point is not publication. Their join point is the return decision, because the corpus treats closure as end-capsule plus archive plus reseed, not as mere termination.
[P2295] B_pair.00 packet
[P2296] L5Case:
[P2297] id: "B_pair.00@l5"
[P2298] suite: "contradiction-plus-replay-coupled"
[P2299] sigma_spine: ["AppA", "AppI", "AppM"]
[P2300] branches:
[P2301] contradiction_branch:
[P2302] district_route: ["M_XV", "H_XYV"]
[P2303] perturbation: "merge-collision between incompatible claim packets"
[P2304] lawful_outputs:

[P2306] fail_path: ["AppK"]

[P2308] district_route: ["A_ZWV"]
[P2309] perturbation: "exact replay drift on a shared route family"

[P2312] fail_path: ["AppK"]
[P2313] join_rule:
[P2314] join_zone: "return-facing decision surface"
[P2315] terminal_organs: ["AppK", "AppP"]
[P2316] terminal_outcomes:
[P2317] - "hold_ambig"
[P2318] - "hold_near"
[P2319] - "quarantine"
[P2320] - "reseed"
[P2321] This is a lawful compound because the docs already define packetized transport, bridge calculus, replay calculus, failure typing, quarantine, runtime repair, publication discipline, and end-capsule return as one connected metabolism rather than isolated features.
[P2322] The first direct reseed rule
[P2323] The first sharp escalation rule is:
[P2324] [\boxed{\mathrm{DirectReseed}\iff(\tau_{\mathrm{contr}}=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_{\mathrm{replay}}=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\mathrm{SharedLineage}=1)\land(\mathrm{RepairClosed}=0)\land(\mathrm{Frontier}\neq\varnothing).}]
[P2325] This is the strongest rule the current corpus supports. It is not saying “any failure means reseed.” It is saying reseed only when contradiction has already crossed into FAIL, replay has also broken beyond bounded repair, both failures belong to the same seed or route family, runtime repair cannot re-close exact replay, and the closure object still carries a nonempty unresolved frontier worth exporting into the next epoch. That last clause matters because the return chapters explicitly define lawful closure as preserving identity, support, unresolved frontier, and return capability, and they explicitly state that reseeding converts that frontier into future work packets.
[P2326] A slightly more operational form is:
[P2327] [\boxed{\mathrm{Quarantine};\text{is sufficient if failure is local;}\qquad\mathrm{Reseed};\text{is required if failure corrupts both adjudication and replay closure of the same lineage.}}]
[P2328] That distinction is not arbitrary. The contradiction branch alone can still remain a lawful AMBIG or a quarantined local FAIL. The replay branch alone can still remain a lawful NEAR with residuals or a quarantined replay break. Direct reseed only becomes the right move when both failures couple and therefore ordinary quarantine would freeze the very lineage that Chapter 15 says must be carried forward as a closure-to-seed object rather than falsely finalized.
[P2329] The exact branch logic
[P2330] The contradiction side still keeps its earlier lawful split:
[P2331] [\mathrm{WitnessGap}\to\mathrm{AMBIGPack}\to\mathrm{AppL},\qquad\mathrm{ReplayMismatch\ or\ irreducible\ contradiction}\to\mathrm{FAILPack}\to\mathrm{AppK}.]
[P2332] The replay side also keeps its earlier lawful split:
[P2333] [\mathrm{corridor\ replay\ preserved}\to\mathrm{NEAR}\to\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM},\qquad\mathrm{corridor\ replay\ broken}\to\mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{FAIL}\to\mathrm{AppK}.]
[P2334] Those two local laws are already fixed by the truth lattice, replay kernel, residual workbench, runtime repair, and quarantine bay. B_pair.00 does not replace them; it composes them.
[P2335] The join condition
[P2336] The new join condition is where the actual lift happens:
[P2337] [\boxed{\bigl(\mathrm{FAIL}{\mathrm{contr}}\in\mathrm{AppK}\bigr);\bowtie;\bigl(\mathrm{FAIL}{\mathrm{replay}}\in\mathrm{AppK}\bigr);\Longrightarrow;\mathrm{AppP\ evaluation}.}]
[P2338] Why AppP and not only AppK? Because the appendix and return chapters distinguish local failure isolation from lawful epoch closure. AppK is the failure / quarantine bay. AppP is deployment, monitoring, final return, and regenerative return. The corpus therefore already implies that once a failure is both contradiction-grade and replay-grade on a shared lineage, the right next question is no longer merely “can this be isolated?” but “must this lineage now close into an end-capsule and emit a successor seed?”
[P2339] The first reseed packet
[P2340] So the correct first emitted reseed object for this compound case is:
[P2341] SuccessorSeedCapsule:
[P2342] id: "reseed.B_pair.00"
[P2343] lineage_ref: "seed://storm.00 + seed://replay.00"

[P2350] unresolved_frontier:
[P2351] - "which branch law or witness condition caused the coupled break"
[P2352] - "whether alternate bridge route exists"
[P2353] - "whether a new seed can separate the two burdens earlier"
[P2354] replay_join_ref: "required-but-not-closed"
[P2355] return_key: "AppP.required"
[P2356] emission_rule: "emit successor seed only because quarantine alone would freeze a still-generative frontier"
[P2357] This packet shape is directly supported by the end-capsule / seed-archive / return protocol material and by the replay and quarantine chapters that already require typed failure objects, unresolved frontier law, and return-ready closure artifacts.
[P2358] The one-line promotion law
[P2359] The one-line law we can now freeze is:
[P2360] [\boxed{(\mathrm{ContradictionFail}\land \mathrm{ReplayFail}\land \mathrm{SharedLineage}\land \neg\mathrm{RepairClosed})\Rightarrow\mathrm{Reseed}\ \text{iff the frontier remains generative.}}]
[P2361] That final frontier clause is the crucial correction. Without it, the system would reseed every catastrophic failure and lose the distinction between dead debris and living unresolved curvature. The corpus explicitly avoids that mistake by defining closure as preserving unresolved frontier and by making the organism remain open rather than falsely final.
[P2362] Why this is the right next move
[P2363] This compound harness pair is the first place where the immune compiler stops looking like separate subsystems and starts behaving like one organism. Contradiction alone is not enough. Replay drift alone is not enough. But contradiction plus replay break on the same lineage produces a genuinely higher-order injury: the organism no longer trusts either its adjudication path or its memory-closure path for that branch. That is exactly the class of event that the return nucleus exists to metabolize into lawful rebirth rather than indefinite frozen quarantine.
[P2364] The strongest next move is to instantiate the third member of the triad, B_seed.00, so the full chain becomes concrete end to end:
[P2365] [B_{\mathrm{storm}.00};\bowtie;B_{\mathrm{replay}.00};\Rightarrow;B_{\mathrm{seed}.00}.]
[P2366] That would let us show the exact end-capsule, frontier ledger, and successor-seed emission path rather than only naming the reseed rule.
[P2367] Concrete specimen — B_seed.00
[P2368] This is the third member of the triad and the first return-nucleus specimen. The corpus is explicit that the return nucleus handles final compression, open-front preservation, next-seed emission, and re-entry into the kernel, while the return current (J_{\mathrm{ret}}) carries public shell objects, shared-law coherence, release trust, and successor-seed packets. In parallel, the mycelial/return texts define lawful closure as an end-capsule that preserves identity, support, unresolved frontier, and return capability, and they define reseeding as converting that frontier into future work packets. The appendix rail then makes the deepest loop explicit: AppP → SeedSummary → AppA.
[P2369] So the lawful concrete route is:
[P2370] [\boxed{B_{\mathrm{seed}.00}:\mathcal S_{XZWV}\to\mathcal D_\star\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA} & \text{lawful successor seed} \\mathrm{ReentryBlock} & \text{return contract fails}\end{cases}}]
[P2371] This is the right chamber route because (\mathcal S_{XZWV}) is the deepest nontrivial surgical line, (\mathcal D_\star) is the unique apex seal, and the return docs consistently treat AppP as the deployment/monitoring/final-return organ rather than a generic archive bucket.
[P2372] Trigger condition
[P2373] B_seed.00 should be entered from B_pair.00, not from arbitrary local failure. The trigger is the coupled condition we already derived:
[P2374] [\boxed{(\mathrm{ContradictionFail}\land \mathrm{ReplayFail}\land \mathrm{SharedLineage}\land \neg\mathrm{RepairClosed}\land \mathrm{Frontier}\neq\varnothing)\RightarrowB_{\mathrm{seed}.00}.}]
[P2375] That aligns with the corpus-wide distinction between ordinary quarantine and regenerative return: quarantine is enough for local containable failure, but once the same lineage loses both adjudication integrity and replay closure, the return loop becomes the lawful next question.

[P2425] Branch A — lawful successor seed
[P2426] The healthy branch is not “everything succeeded.” It is: closure is acknowledged as failed at the object level, but the failure has been compressed into a lawful end-capsule that still preserves identity and a generative unresolved frontier, and the return nucleus can emit a successor seed back into the kernel. The docs are unusually clear that closure is not death but end-capsule, archive, reseed, and lawful rebirth, and that the return nucleus specifically performs final compression, open-front preservation, next-seed emission, and re-entry into the kernel.
