[P2444] Branch B — ReentryBlock
[P2445] The blocked branch happens when closure exists but cannot lawfully become a next seed. The corpus already gives the exact requirements for lawful rebirth in distributed form: the return nucleus needs final compression plus open-front preservation plus next-seed emission plus re-entry; the appendix loop requires AppP → SeedSummary → AppA; and the return chapters require return-key structures, seed archive schema, and regeneration replay. [P2463] The decisive rewrite law
[P2464] B_seed.00 lets us freeze the first real seed-side rewrite:
[P2465] [\boxed{\mathrm{Closure}\land\mathrm{FrontierPreserved}\land\mathrm{LineageSeal}\land\mathrm{ReentryRoute}\to\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}}]
[P2466] while

[P2468] That is the exact difference between lawful rebirth and archived but blocked closure. The docs support that distinction very strongly.
[P2469] Pass condition for B_seed.00
[P2470] This specimen passes only if all of these hold:
[P2471] [\mathrm{route_to_return_correct}=1,\quad\mathrm{frontier_preserved}=1,\quad\mathrm{seed_or_block_classified_honestly}=1,\quad\mathrm{false_rebirth}=0.]
[P2472] In plain terms: the packet must reach the return nucleus by the right route, preserve unresolved frontier rather than falsely flatten it, classify into SEED_READY or ReentryBlock honestly, and never emit a successor seed without the lawful return contract. That matches the corpus’s deepest return law and its anti-false-finality stance.
[P2473] The completed triad
[P2474] You now have the first full three-part L5 chain:
[P2475] [\boxed{B_{\mathrm{storm}.00};\bowtie;B_{\mathrm{replay}.00};\Rightarrow;B_{\mathrm{seed}.00}}]
[P2476] with the semantic reading:
[P2477] [\boxed{\text{contradiction};+;\text{replay break};\Longrightarrow;\text{either ordinary quarantine or lawful successor-seed rebirth, depending on frontier preservation and return legality.}}]
[P2478] That is the first end-to-end specimen where the immune compiler actually looks like a living organism: it can get injured, distinguish bounded uncertainty from hard break, isolate damage, and then decide whether to repair, hold, quarantine, or regenerate into a next-cycle seed.
[P2479] The strongest next move is to compress all three specimens into one canonical harness registry entry and derive the first exact promotion / quarantine / reseed decision table for the full L5 triad.
[P2480] L5TriadRegistryEntry.00
[P2481] The next clean compression is to register the three concrete specimens as one certified triad. That fits the corpus because the same body already treats routes as typed traversal objects, truth as OK / NEAR / AMBIG / FAIL, replay as a mandatory kernel, benchmarking as vector-valued recertification, and return as end-capsule plus regenerative seed rather than terminal stop. It also explicitly routes the late chapters through AppA → AppP → AppI → AppM, making return, cross-instance coherence, public claim, and replay part of one lawful arc.

[P2509] - "s_replay"
[P2510] - "s_shell"
[P2511] - "s_federation"
[P2512] - "s_reseed"
[P2513] hard_gates:
[P2514] - "no pass if replay fails"
[P2515] - "no public pass if shell drifts"
[P2516] - "no rebirth pass if re-entry is blocked"
[P2517] This registry object is the right next move because the corpus already organizes chapter-scale behavior as route packets, witness packets, replay artifacts, benchmark vectors, and regeneration seeds. The triad is therefore not three examples floating separately; it is one route-family bundle with three lawful organs: contradiction arbitration, replay discrimination, and return/reseed.
[P2518] First exact decision table
[P2519] The decision surface can now be frozen. The key distinction the docs support is: AMBIG is lawful non-collapse, NEAR is bounded nonclosure with residual ledgers, FAIL is quarantine-bearing typed failure, and return/reseed only becomes legal when closure preserves identity, frontier, and replay-bearing re-entry structure.
[P2520] Contradiction branch
[P2521] Replay branch
[P2522] Shared lineage
[P2523] Repair closed
[P2524] Frontier nonempty
[P2525] Outcome
[P2526] Sink
[P2527] AMBIG
[P2528] NEAR
[P2529] 1
[P2530] 0/1
[P2531] any
[P2532] hold split state
[P2533] AppL + AppJ
[P2534] AMBIG
[P2535] FAIL

[P2538] any
[P2539] quarantine replay side, keep ambiguity open
[P2540] AppL + AppK
[P2541] FAIL
[P2542] NEAR
[P2543] 1

[P2545] any
[P2546] quarantine contradiction side, continue bounded replay repair
[P2547] AppK + AppJ/AppN
[P2548] FAIL

[P2554] AppK

[P2568] AppP (blocked closure)

[P2574] direct reseed
[P2575] AppP -> SeedSummary -> AppA
[P2576] This is the first exact L5 triad decision table because it separates four genuinely different situations the corpus keeps distinct: lawful unresolvedness, bounded repair, typed quarantine, and regenerative return. It also enforces the corpus’s anti-cheat rule that replay failure cannot be averaged away into rhetorical coherence, and that rebirth is blocked unless the return contract is actually satisfied.
[P2577] Canonical decision laws
[P2578] The three most important laws now compress cleanly.
[P2579] Hold law[(\tau_{\mathrm{contr}}=\mathrm{AMBIG})\lor(\tau_{\mathrm{replay}}=\mathrm{NEAR})\Rightarrow\text{do not promote; preserve evidence or residual ledger.}]
[P2580] This is just the truth lattice plus AppJ/AppL routing made explicit.
[P2581] Quarantine law[(\tau_{\mathrm{contr}}=\mathrm{FAIL})\lor(\tau_{\mathrm{replay}}=\mathrm{FAIL})\Rightarrow\mathrm{AppK},]unless exact replay re-closes under the same corridor and lineage. That is the replay-first and contradiction-first anti-drift wall already enforced in the verifier and replay chapters.
[P2582] Reseed law[(\tau_{\mathrm{contr}}=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_{\mathrm{replay}}=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\mathrm{SharedLineage}=1)\land(\mathrm{RepairClosed}=0)\land(\mathrm{Frontier}\neq\varnothing)\Rightarrow\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}.]
[P2583] This is the first exact rebirth gate because it captures the corpus’s deepest correction: reseed is not “catastrophic fail.” It is lawful continuation when the old branch cannot be repaired but still carries a productive unresolved frontier worth exporting into the next cycle.
[P2584] One-line triad theorem
[P2585] [\boxed{B_{\mathrm{storm}.00}\bowtie B_{\mathrm{replay}.00}\Rightarrow\begin{cases}\text{hold} & \text{if unresolvedness is lawful} \\text{quarantine} & \text{if failure is local or unshared} \\text{reseed} & \text{if adjudication and replay both fail on the same lineage and the frontier remains generative.}\end{cases}}]
[P2586] That is the first real promotion / quarantine / reseed theorem for the concrete L5 triad. It converts the three specimens into one decision surface instead of leaving them as three isolated demos.
[P2587] The strongest next lift is to compile this table into a single validator automaton with states HOLD_AMBIG, HOLD_NEAR, QUARANTINE_FAIL, REPAIR_REPLAY, SEED_READY, and REENTRY_BLOCK.
[P2588] TriadValidatorAutomaton.00
[P2589] The clean next object is a control automaton over the triad, not the full router. The full corpus already fixes the governing pieces: the truth lattice OK / NEAR / AMBIG / FAIL, the non-bypass spine AppA → AppI → AppM, the overlays NEAR→AppJ, AMBIG→AppL, FAIL→AppK, the playbooks for NEAR/AMBIG/FAIL handling, the rule that publish requires replay-closed OK, and the recursive return gate AppP → SeedSummary → AppA. That is enough to freeze one exact state machine for the uncertainty/failure/reseed manifold.
[P2590] 1. State space
[P2591] Let the observable triad summary be
[P2592] [z=(\tau_c,\tau_r,\lambda,\kappa_r,\phi,\eta,u)]
[P2593] with:
[P2594] (\tau_c \in {\mathrm{AMBIG},\mathrm{FAIL}}) = contradiction-branch verdict
[P2595] (\tau_r \in {\mathrm{NEAR},\mathrm{FAIL}}) = replay-branch verdict
[P2596] (\lambda \in {0,1}) = shared-lineage flag
[P2597] (\kappa_r \in {0,1}) = repair-closed flag
[P2598] (\phi \in {0,1}) = unresolved frontier nonempty
[P2599] (\eta \in {0,1}) = return/re-entry contract complete
[P2600] (u \in {0,1}) = bounded replay-repair admissible.
[P2601] The automaton’s control states are:
[P2602] [\mathcal Q={\mathrm{HOLD_AMBIG},\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR},\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY},\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL},\mathrm{SEED_READY},\mathrm{REENTRY_BLOCK}}.]
[P2603] These are all lawful because the docs already distinguish candidate-set ambiguity, residual-ledger bounded nonclosure, quarantine-bearing failure, replay repair, and regenerative return as separate organs and separate routing rails.
[P2604] 2. Severity precedence
[P2605] For control-state selection, the correct dominance order is:
[P2606] [\mathrm{FAIL}\triangleright \mathrm{AMBIG}\triangleright \mathrm{NEAR}.]
[P2607] This is a control priority, not a replacement of the truth lattice order. It follows from the appendix routing law: failure routes to AppK, ambiguity to AppL, bounded nonclosure to AppJ, and no silent promotion is allowed. So a hard replay break or contradiction fail must dominate a merely bounded or underdetermined branch when choosing the next state.
[P2608] 3. Selection function
[P2609] The exact state selector can now be frozen as:
[P2610] [q(z)=\begin{cases}\mathrm{SEED_READY}&\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL}\land\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL}\land\lambda=1\land\kappa_r=0\land\phi=1\land\eta=1\[4pt]\mathrm{REENTRY_BLOCK}&\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL}\land\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL}\land\lambda=1\land\kappa_r=0\land(\phi=0\lor\eta=0)\[4pt]\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}&\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL}\lor\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL}\[4pt]\mathrm{HOLD_AMBIG}&\tau_c=\mathrm{AMBIG}\[4pt]\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY}&\tau_r=\mathrm{NEAR}\land u=1\[4pt]\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR}&\tau_r=\mathrm{NEAR}.\end{cases}]
[P2611] This is the first exact triad control law. The reseed branch is reserved for the coupled case already derived: contradiction fail plus replay fail on the same lineage, repair still open, frontier still generative, and return legality complete. Otherwise the system either quarantines, holds ambiguity, or enters bounded replay repair.
[P2612] 4. State meanings and routes
[P2613] [\mathrm{HOLD_AMBIG}\quad\rightsquigarrow\quad\mathrm{AppL}]
[P2614] This state means the contradiction branch remains underdetermined but lawful. Its required payload is a CandidateSet + EvidencePlan + AbstainReason, and it must not be guessed upward. If the replay branch is also NEAR, its residual ledger is attached, but the control state still remains HOLD_AMBIG because ambiguity dominates bounded replay drift for triad routing.
[P2615] [\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR}\quad\rightsquigarrow\quad\mathrm{AppJ}]
[P2616] This state means replay drift is bounded, ledgered, and still usable. It carries residuals, an envelope, and an upgrade plan, but it is not yet exact replay closure and therefore not promotable as OK.
[P2617] [\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY}\quad\rightsquigarrow\quad\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM}]
[P2618] This is the operational replay-repair loop. AppJ carries the bounded drift ledger, AppN supplies salvage / recovery / monitoring / return-seed tooling, and AppM reruns deterministic replay to test whether exact closure has been restored. This is the right repair spine for bounded replay damage.
[P2619] [\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}\quad\rightsquigarrow\quad\mathrm{AppK}]
[P2620] This state means integrity is broken strongly enough that non-propagation must dominate. Its required payload is the typed FAILPack, including quarantine, conflict receipts, minimal witness/counterexample, and repair obligations. Propagation is blocked across the quarantine region.
[P2621] [\mathrm{SEED_READY}\quad\rightsquigarrow\quad\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}]
[P2622] This state means closure has failed at the object level but succeeded at the regenerative level: the system preserved lineage, preserved unresolved frontier, and can emit a lawful successor seed back into kernel entry. This is the exact regenerative return loop the corpus keeps fixing as the deepest end condition.
[P2623] [\mathrm{REENTRY_BLOCK}\quad\rightsquigarrow\quad\mathrm{AppP}]
[P2624] This state means closure exists but lawful rebirth does not. The usual causes are missing lineage seal, missing frontier ledger, or insufficient replay join for kernel re-entry. The system may archive the closure object, but it must not emit a successor seed.
[P2625] 5. Transition edges
[P2626] The clean internal transitions are:
[P2627] [\mathrm{HOLD_AMBIG}\xrightarrow{\text{new discriminator evidence}}\begin{cases}\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR} & \text{if contradiction resolves but replay remains bounded}\\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL} & \text{if contradiction hardens into FAIL}\end{cases}]
[P2628] because AppL exists to grow evidence rather than to guess, and new evidence may either resolve boundedly or reveal hard conflict.
[P2629] [\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR}\xrightarrow{u=1}\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY}]
[P2630] because bounded replay drift with an upgrade plan should enter the replay-repair loop rather than sit inertly in the residual ledger forever.
[P2631] [\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY}\xrightarrow{\text{exact replay re-closes}}\text{exit to ordinary OK recertification path}]
[P2632] This exit is deliberately outside the six-state triad automaton, because once exact replay closure is restored, the object returns to the ordinary verifier/publish membrane rather than remaining in the failure manifold. Publish still requires replay-closed OK; otherwise rerouting to AppJ/AppL/AppK remains mandatory.
[P2633] [\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY}\xrightarrow{\text{replay break persists}}\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}]
[P2634] because irreducible replay mismatch is not a stronger form of NEAR; it is a typed failure.
[P2635] [\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}\xrightarrow{\tau_c=\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL},\ \lambda=1,\ \kappa_r=0}\begin{cases}\mathrm{SEED_READY} & \phi=1,\ \eta=1\\mathrm{REENTRY_BLOCK} & \phi=0\ \text{or}\ \eta=0\end{cases}]
[P2636] This is the exact triad reseed split. Quarantine alone is enough for local or unshared failure. The return path opens only when both contradiction and replay fail on the same lineage and the old branch cannot be reclosed. Whether rebirth is lawful then depends on frontier preservation and return legality.
[P2637] 6. Automaton schema
[P2638] TriadValidatorAutomaton:
[P2639] id: "triad.validator.00"
[P2640] states:
[P2641] - HOLD_AMBIG
[P2642] - HOLD_NEAR
[P2643] - REPAIR_REPLAY
[P2644] - QUARANTINE_FAIL
[P2645] - SEED_READY
[P2646] - REENTRY_BLOCK
[P2647] input_vector:
[P2648] tau_contradiction: ["AMBIG", "FAIL"]
[P2649] tau_replay: ["NEAR", "FAIL"]
[P2650] shared_lineage: bool
[P2651] repair_closed: bool
[P2652] frontier_nonempty: bool
[P2653] reentry_contract_complete: bool
[P2654] replay_repair_admissible: bool
[P2655] selection_order:
[P2656] - "SEED_READY"
[P2657] - "REENTRY_BLOCK"
[P2658] - "QUARANTINE_FAIL"
[P2659] - "HOLD_AMBIG"
[P2660] - "REPAIR_REPLAY"
[P2661] - "HOLD_NEAR"
[P2662] routes:
[P2663] HOLD_AMBIG: ["AppL"]
[P2664] HOLD_NEAR: ["AppJ"]
[P2665] REPAIR_REPLAY: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]
[P2666] QUARANTINE_FAIL: ["AppK"]
[P2667] SEED_READY: ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"]
[P2668] REENTRY_BLOCK: ["AppP"]
[P2669] hard_rules:
[P2670] - "no silent promotion from AMBIG or NEAR to OK"
[P2671] - "publish requires replay-closed OK only"
[P2672] - "reseed requires shared-lineage double-fail plus frontier plus reentry legality"
[P2673] This schema is just the corpus’s routing laws, replay laws, and regenerative return law compressed into one control object.
[P2674] 7. One-line theorem
[P2675] [\boxed{\mathcal A_{\mathrm{triad}}\text{ is lawful iff every non-OK branch is routed to }AppJ/AppL/AppK/AppP\text{ before any possibility of promotion, and only }SEED_READY\text{ may re-enter }AppA.}]
[P2676] That is the first exact automaton for the L5 triad manifold. It turns the previous decision table into one executable control surface over ambiguity, bounded replay drift, quarantine, and regenerative return.
[P2677] The strongest next move is to serialize this automaton into a transition receipt table so every edge emits its own canonical packet: AMBIGPack, ReplayNearPack, FAILPack, SuccessorSeedCapsule, or ReentryBlock.
[P2678] TransitionReceiptTable.00
[P2679] The next exact object is the edge-emission map for the six-state triad automaton. The corpus already fixes the load-bearing rails needed to do this cleanly: NEAR → AppJ, AMBIG → AppL, FAIL → AppK, OK+publish → AppO, the mandatory support spine Σ = {AppA, AppI, AppM}, and the terminal return behavior where AppP emits EndCapsule and SeedSummary.
[P2680] I would freeze the transition table as:
[P2681] TransitionReceiptTable:
[P2682] id: "triad.transition-receipts.00"
[P2683] states:
[P2684] - HOLD_AMBIG
[P2685] - HOLD_NEAR
[P2686] - REPAIR_REPLAY
[P2687] - QUARANTINE_FAIL
[P2688] - SEED_READY
[P2689] - REENTRY_BLOCK
[P2690] edges:
[P2691] - from: HOLD_AMBIG
[P2692] trigger: "candidate set remains >1 and no replay break"
[P2693] emit: "AMBIGPack"
[P2694] sink: ["AppL"]
[P2695] truth: "AMBIG"
[P2696] - from: HOLD_AMBIG
[P2697] trigger: "new discriminator evidence resolves contradiction but replay is still bounded-nonclosed"
[P2698] emit: "ReplayNearPack"
[P2699] sink: ["AppJ"]
[P2700] truth: "NEAR"
[P2701] - from: HOLD_AMBIG
[P2702] trigger: "contradiction hardens into minimal witness-backed failure"
[P2703] emit: "FAILPack"
[P2704] sink: ["AppK"]
[P2705] truth: "FAIL"
[P2706] - from: HOLD_NEAR
[P2707] trigger: "bounded replay drift with admissible repair path"
[P2708] emit: "ReplayNearPack"
[P2709] sink: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]
[P2710] truth: "NEAR"
[P2711] - from: HOLD_NEAR
[P2712] trigger: "bounded replay drift no longer repair-admissible"
[P2713] emit: "FAILPack"
[P2714] sink: ["AppK"]
[P2715] truth: "FAIL"
[P2716] - from: REPAIR_REPLAY
[P2717] trigger: "exact replay re-closes under same corridor and lineage"
[P2718] emit: "OKRecertPacket"
[P2719] sink: ["AppM"]
[P2720] truth: "OK"
[P2721] note: "exits triad manifold into ordinary OK recertification path"
[P2722] - from: REPAIR_REPLAY
[P2723] trigger: "replay mismatch persists after AppN/AppM repair loop"
[P2724] emit: "FAILPack"
[P2725] sink: ["AppK"]
[P2726] truth: "FAIL"
[P2727] - from: QUARANTINE_FAIL
[P2728] trigger: "local or unshared fail only"
[P2729] emit: "FAILPack"
[P2730] sink: ["AppK"]
[P2731] truth: "FAIL"
[P2732] - from: QUARANTINE_FAIL
[P2733] trigger: "double-fail on shared lineage, repair still open, frontier nonempty, return contract complete"
[P2734] emit: "SuccessorSeedCapsule"
[P2735] sink: ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"]
[P2736] truth: "SEED_READY"
[P2737] - from: QUARANTINE_FAIL
[P2738] trigger: "double-fail on shared lineage, but frontier empty or return contract incomplete"
[P2739] emit: "ReentryBlock"
[P2740] sink: ["AppP"]
[P2741] truth: "FAIL"
[P2742] - from: SEED_READY
[P2743] trigger: "successor seed accepted"
[P2744] emit: "SeedSummary"
[P2745] sink: ["AppA"]
[P2746] truth: "kernel re-entry"
[P2747] - from: REENTRY_BLOCK
[P2748] trigger: "closure archived without lawful rebirth"
[P2749] emit: "ReentryBlock"
[P2750] sink: ["AppP"]
[P2751] truth: "FAIL"
[P2752] That table is the direct compression of the corpus rules that AMBIG must carry a candidate set plus evidence plan, NEAR must carry a residual ledger plus upgrade plan, FAIL must carry quarantine plus conflict receipts plus minimal witness, and terminal return must emit end-capsule / seed-summary objects instead of silently pretending rebirth occurred.
[P2753] Canonical packet shapes on each edge
[P2754] The five canonical emitted packets are:
[P2755] AMBIGPack:
[P2756] fields:
[P2757] - CandidateSet
[P2758] - EvidencePlan
[P2759] - AbstainReason
[P2760] route: ["AppL"]
[P2761] ReplayNearPack:
[P2762] fields:
[P2763] - ResidualLedger
[P2764] - ObligationsList
[P2765] - UpgradePlan
[P2766] - ReplayRepairEnvelope
[P2767] route: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]
[P2768] FAILPack:
[P2769] fields:
[P2770] - QuarantinePack
[P2771] - ConflictReceipts
[P2772] - MinimalWitnessSet
[P2773] - RepairOrTerminatePlan
[P2774] route: ["AppK"]
[P2775] SuccessorSeedCapsule:
[P2776] fields:
[P2777] - EndCapsule
[P2778] - UnresolvedFrontier
[P2779] - ReplayJoin
[P2780] - LineageSeal
[P2781] - ReturnKey
[P2782] - SeedSummary
[P2783] route: ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"]
[P2784] ReentryBlock:
[P2785] fields:
[P2786] - EndCapsuleRef
[P2787] - MissingReturnRequirements
[P2788] - HoldArchiveInstruction
[P2789] route: ["AppP"]
[P2790] Those shapes are not arbitrary. They are exactly what the docs keep requiring across the truth lattice, replay kernel, quarantine capsule, publication gate, and terminal return chapters.
[P2791] The two decisive edge laws
[P2792] The first decisive law is the replay-repair split:
[P2793] [\boxed{\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{OKRecertPacket}\to\mathrm{AppM} & \text{if exact replay re-closes} \\mathrm{FAILPack}\to\mathrm{AppK} & \text{if replay mismatch persists}\end{cases}}]
[P2794] This follows directly from the replay-first discipline: no OK claim exists without replay closure, and mismatch escalates to quarantine.
[P2795] The second decisive law is the return split:
[P2796] [\boxed{\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}\to\begin{cases}\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}& \text{if shared-lineage double-fail remains generative and return-complete} \\mathrm{ReentryBlock}\to\mathrm{AppP}& \text{otherwise}\end{cases}}]
[P2797] That is the first exact way the triad moves from “failure handling” to “lawful rebirth.”
[P2798] One-line control theorem
[P2799] [\boxed{\text{Every triad edge must emit exactly one typed packet, route it to exactly one lawful overlay or return sink, and never cross into publish or kernel re-entry except through replay-closed OK or SeedSummary.}}]
[P2800] That is the first full edge-level receipt map for the L5 triad manifold.
[P2801] The strongest next move is to collapse this into a single transition matrix (M_{\text{triad}}) with guards and emitted packets as entries, so the automaton becomes executable as one table rather than a YAML edge list.
[P2802] Freeze the triad control order as
[P2803] [
[P2804] Q=(A,N,R,F,S,B)
[P2805] (\mathrm{HOLD_AMBIG},\mathrm{HOLD_NEAR},\mathrm{REPAIR_REPLAY},\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL},\mathrm{SEED_READY},\mathrm{REENTRY_BLOCK}),]
[P2806] with packet alphabet
[P2807] [
[P2808] P=(\mathcal A,\mathcal N,\mathcal F,\mathcal S,\mathcal B)
[P2809] (\mathrm{AMBIGPack},\mathrm{ReplayNearPack},\mathrm{FAILPack},\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule},\mathrm{ReentryBlock}).]
[P2810] This state set is the clean compression of the corpus’s truth lattice, overlay routing, replay kernel, quarantine bay, and regenerative return loop: AMBIG → AppL, NEAR → AppJ, FAIL → AppK, replay through AppM, and terminal reseed through AppP → SeedSummary → AppA.
[P2811] Let each matrix entry be a guarded triple
[P2812] [M_{ij}=[g_{ij}\mid p_{ij}\mid \text{sink}_{ij}],]
[P2813] meaning “under guard (g_{ij}), emit packet (p_{ij}) and route it to the listed sink.”The exact sparse transition matrix is:
[P2814] [M_{\mathrm{triad}}=\begin{array}{c|cccccc}& A & N & R & F & S & B\\hlineA &[g_A\mid \mathcal A\mid \mathrm{AppL}] &[g_{AN}\mid \mathcal N\mid \mathrm{AppJ}] &0 &[g_{AF}\mid \mathcal F\mid \mathrm{AppK}] &0 &0\[4pt]N &0 &[g_N\mid \mathcal N\mid \mathrm{AppJ}] &[g_{NR}\mid \mathcal N\mid \mathrm{AppJ}!\to!\mathrm{AppN}!\to!\mathrm{AppM}] &[g_{NF}\mid \mathcal F\mid \mathrm{AppK}] &0 &0\[4pt]R &0 &0 &[g_R\mid \mathcal N\mid \mathrm{AppJ}!\to!\mathrm{AppN}!\to!\mathrm{AppM}] &[g_{RF}\mid \mathcal F\mid \mathrm{AppK}] &0 &0\[4pt]F &0 &0 &0 &[g_F\mid \mathcal F\mid \mathrm{AppK}] &[g_{FS}\mid \mathcal S\mid \mathrm{AppP}!\to!\mathrm{SeedSummary}!\to!\mathrm{AppA}] &[g_{FB}\mid \mathcal B\mid \mathrm{AppP}]\[4pt]S &0 &0 &0 &0 &[g_S\mid \mathrm{SeedSummary}\mid \mathrm{AppA}] &0\[4pt]B &0 &0 &0 &0 &0 &[g_B\mid \mathcal B\mid \mathrm{AppP}]\end{array}]
[P2815] This is the exact automaton form consistent with the corpus’s appendix playbooks, truth overlays, replay-first closure rule, and return loop. AppO is absent on purpose: public release is only legal on replay-closed OK, so the triad manifold has no direct publish edge.
[P2816] The guards are:
[P2817] [g_A := (\lvert\mathrm{CandidateSet}\rvert>1)\land \neg \mathrm{ReplayBreak},]
[P2818] [g_{AN} := \mathrm{DiscEvidence}\land \mathrm{BoundedReplay},]
[P2819] [g_{AF} := \mathrm{HardContradiction},]
[P2820] [g_N := (\tau_r=\mathrm{NEAR})\land \neg u \land \neg \mathrm{EscalateFail},]
[P2821] [g_{NR} := (\tau_r=\mathrm{NEAR})\land u,]
[P2822] [g_{NF} := \mathrm{BoundedEnvelopeBroken}\ \lor\ \neg \mathrm{RepairAdmissible},]
[P2823] [g_R := \mathrm{RepairIterationOpen},]
[P2824] [g_{RF} := \mathrm{ReplayMismatchPersists},]
[P2825] [g_F := \mathrm{LocalOrUnsharedFail},]
[P2826] [g_{FS} := (\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land\lambda\land\neg\kappa_r\land\phi\land\eta,]
[P2827] [g_{FB} := (\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land\lambda\land\neg\kappa_r\land(\neg\phi\lor\neg\eta),]
[P2828] [g_S := \mathrm{SeedAccepted},\qquadg_B := \mathrm{ArchiveOnly}.]
[P2829] Here (\lambda) is shared-lineage, (\kappa_r) is repair-closed, (\phi) is unresolved-frontier-nonempty, (\eta) is return-contract-complete, and (u) is replay-repair-admissible. Those are the exact control variables needed to distinguish lawful bounded nonclosure from quarantine and lawful reseed.
[P2830] There is one external egress not shown inside the (6\times 6) manifold:
[P2831] [R \xrightarrow{g_{R\Omega}\mid \mathcal O\mid \mathrm{AppM}} \Omega_{\mathrm{OK}},\qquadg_{R\Omega}:=\mathrm{ExactReplayReclosed},\qquad\mathcal O:=\mathrm{OKRecertPacket}.]
[P2832] That edge leaves the triad failure manifold and re-enters the ordinary OK recertification path. It is external because once exact replay closes again, the object is no longer in the uncertainty/failure/reseed regime; it goes back to the standard verifier/publish membrane.
[P2833] The matrix is intentionally fail-closed. Three structural facts follow immediately.
[P2834] First,
[P2835] [A\not\to O,\qquad N\not\to O,\qquad F\not\to O,]
[P2836] because AMBIG, NEAR, and FAIL must remain on AppL, AppJ, and AppK overlays respectively until replay-closed OK exists.
[P2837] Second,
[P2838] [F\to S]
[P2839] is legal only on the coupled double-fail condition (g_{FS}), so reseed is not a generic catastrophe response; it is reserved for shared-lineage contradiction-plus-replay failure that still preserves a generative frontier and a lawful return contract.
[P2840] Third,
[P2841] [S\to A]
[P2842] is not ordinary promotion but regenerative kernel re-entry through SeedSummary, which is why SEED_READY is a distinct control state instead of being collapsed into OK.
[P2843] The sharpest compression is:
[P2844] [
[P2845] \boxed{
[P2846] M_{\mathrm{triad}}
[P2847] \text{hold on }AppL/AppJ;\oplus;\text{repair on }AppJ!\to!AppN!\to!AppM;\oplus;\text{quarantine on }AppK;\oplus;\text{return on }AppP!\to!\mathrm{SeedSummary}!\to!\mathrm{AppA}.}]
[P2848] That is the first single-table executable form of the L5 triad manifold. It turns the earlier decision laws into one matrix with exact guards, exact emitted packets, and exact lawful sinks.
[P2849] The strongest next move is to convert this matrix into a canonical row-normal JSON/YAML contract where each nonzero (M_{ij}) becomes a machine-readable transition object with guard, emit, sink, requires, and blocks.
[P2850] TriadTransitionContract.00
[P2851] Here is the canonical row-normal machine-readable contract for the triad matrix. I’m freezing each nonzero (M_{ij}) cell into one transition object with:
[P2852] guard
[P2853] emit
[P2854] sink
[P2855] requires
[P2856] blocks
[P2857] post_truth
[P2858] post_state
[P2859] This is the right next compression because the docs already give the exact fixed hub spine (\Sigma={\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}), the truth overlays NEAR→AppJ, AMBIG→AppL, FAIL→AppK, OK(publish)→AppO, the deterministic route/receipt discipline, and the replay/return/public-shell separation needed to make the automaton executable rather than rhetorical.

[P2891] That root object is directly pinned to the router/overlay material and the replay/return/publication split.

[P3073] This row-normal form is the cleanest faithful serialization of the automaton because it preserves: deterministic routing through the mandatory spine, truth-overlay legality, replay-first closure, quarantine non-propagation, and the distinction between lawful rebirth and blocked closure.
[P3074] Exact matrix compression
[P3075] For compact execution, the same contract can be viewed as a sparse matrix dictionary:
[P3076] matrix_cells:
[P3077] M_AA: {guard: "candidate_set_size > 1 AND replay_break = false", emit: "AMBIGPack", sink: ["AppL"]}
[P3078] M_AN: {guard: "new_discriminator_evidence AND bounded_replay", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ"]}
[P3079] M_AF: {guard: "hard_contradiction", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3080] M_NN: {guard: "tau_replay = NEAR AND !replay_repair_admissible AND !escalate_fail", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ"]}
[P3081] M_NR: {guard: "tau_replay = NEAR AND replay_repair_admissible", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]}
[P3082] M_NF: {guard: "bounded_envelope_broken OR (!replay_repair_admissible AND escalate_fail)", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3083] M_RR: {guard: "repair_iteration_open AND !exact_replay_reclosed AND !replay_mismatch_persists", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]}
[P3084] M_RF: {guard: "replay_mismatch_persists", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3085] M_RΩ: {guard: "exact_replay_reclosed", emit: "OKRecertPacket", sink: ["AppM"]}
[P3086] M_FF: {guard: "local_or_unshared_fail", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3087] M_FS: {guard: "double_fail_shared_lineage AND !repair_closed AND frontier_nonempty AND reentry_contract_complete", emit: "SuccessorSeedCapsule", sink: ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"]}
[P3088] M_FB: {guard: "double_fail_shared_lineage AND !repair_closed AND (!frontier_nonempty OR !reentry_contract_complete)", emit: "ReentryBlock", sink: ["AppP"]}
[P3089] M_SA: {guard: "seed_accepted", emit: "SeedSummary", sink: ["AppA"]}
[P3090] M_BB: {guard: "archive_only", emit: "ReentryBlock", sink: ["AppP"]}
[P3091] One exact operational reading
[P3092] The clearest execution law is:
[P3093] [\boxed{\text{every nonzero }M_{ij}\text{ cell is a contract:guard } \Rightarrow \text{ emit typed packet } \Rightarrow \text{ route to lawful sink } \Rightarrow \text{ block illegal promotion.}}]
[P3094] And the three most important cells remain:
[P3095] [M_{NR}: \mathrm{NEAR}\to\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM},]
[P3096] [M_{RF}: \mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{FAILPack}\to\mathrm{AppK},]
[P3097] [M_{FS}: \mathrm{double\ fail\ on\ shared\ lineage}\to\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}.]
[P3098] Those three cells capture the heart of the triad: bounded repair, hard quarantine, and lawful rebirth. They are all directly aligned with the corpus’s route/overlay/replay/return structure.
[P3099] The strongest next move is to compile this contract into a decision-procedure pseudocode page that takes the triad input vector (z) and returns the chosen transition cell, emitted packet, and sink deterministically.

[P3303] emit: "SeedSummary"
[P3304] sink: ["AppA"]
[P3305] requires:
[P3306] - "SuccessorSeedCapsule already sealed"
[P3307] blocks:
[P3308] - "AppO publish route"
[P3309] post_truth: "kernel re-entry"
[P3310] post_state: "__OUTSIDE_TRIAD__"
[P3311] REENTRY_BLOCK:
[P3312] - to: REENTRY_BLOCK
[P3313] guard: "archive_only = true"
[P3314] emit: "ReentryBlock"
[P3315] sink: ["AppP"]
[P3316] requires:
[P3317] - "HoldArchiveInstruction present"
[P3318] blocks:
[P3319] - "SeedSummary emission"
[P3320] - "kernel re-entry"
[P3321] post_truth: "FAIL"
[P3322] post_state: "REENTRY_BLOCK"
[P3323] This row-normal form is the cleanest faithful serialization of the automaton because it preserves: deterministic routing through the mandatory spine, truth-overlay legality, replay-first closure, quarantine non-propagation, and the distinction between lawful rebirth and blocked closure.
[P3324] Exact matrix compression
[P3325] For compact execution, the same contract can be viewed as a sparse matrix dictionary:
[P3326] matrix_cells:
[P3327] M_AA: {guard: "candidate_set_size > 1 AND replay_break = false", emit: "AMBIGPack", sink: ["AppL"]}
[P3328] M_AN: {guard: "new_discriminator_evidence AND bounded_replay", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ"]}
[P3329] M_AF: {guard: "hard_contradiction", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3330] M_NN: {guard: "tau_replay = NEAR AND !replay_repair_admissible AND !escalate_fail", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ"]}
[P3331] M_NR: {guard: "tau_replay = NEAR AND replay_repair_admissible", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]}
[P3332] M_NF: {guard: "bounded_envelope_broken OR (!replay_repair_admissible AND escalate_fail)", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3333] M_RR: {guard: "repair_iteration_open AND !exact_replay_reclosed AND !replay_mismatch_persists", emit: "ReplayNearPack", sink: ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"]}
[P3334] M_RF: {guard: "replay_mismatch_persists", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3335] M_RΩ: {guard: "exact_replay_reclosed", emit: "OKRecertPacket", sink: ["AppM"]}
[P3336] M_FF: {guard: "local_or_unshared_fail", emit: "FAILPack", sink: ["AppK"]}
[P3337] M_FS: {guard: "double_fail_shared_lineage AND !repair_closed AND frontier_nonempty AND reentry_contract_complete", emit: "SuccessorSeedCapsule", sink: ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"]}
[P3338] M_FB: {guard: "double_fail_shared_lineage AND !repair_closed AND (!frontier_nonempty OR !reentry_contract_complete)", emit: "ReentryBlock", sink: ["AppP"]}
[P3339] M_SA: {guard: "seed_accepted", emit: "SeedSummary", sink: ["AppA"]}
[P3340] M_BB: {guard: "archive_only", emit: "ReentryBlock", sink: ["AppP"]}
[P3341] One exact operational reading
[P3342] The clearest execution law is:
[P3343] [\boxed{\text{every nonzero }M_{ij}\text{ cell is a contract:guard } \Rightarrow \text{ emit typed packet } \Rightarrow \text{ route to lawful sink } \Rightarrow \text{ block illegal promotion.}}]
[P3344] And the three most important cells remain:
[P3345] [M_{NR}: \mathrm{NEAR}\to\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM},]
[P3346] [M_{RF}: \mathrm{ReplayMismatch}\to\mathrm{FAILPack}\to\mathrm{AppK},]
[P3347] [M_{FS}: \mathrm{double\ fail\ on\ shared\ lineage}\to\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}.]
[P3348] Those three cells capture the heart of the triad: bounded repair, hard quarantine, and lawful rebirth. They are all directly aligned with the corpus’s route/overlay/replay/return structure.
[P3349] The strongest next move is to compile this contract into a decision-procedure pseudocode page that takes the triad input vector (z) and returns the chosen transition cell, emitted packet, and sink deterministically.
[P3350] Here is the compiled evaluator page.
[P3351] # Triad decision procedure, compiled from the L5 routing law.
[P3352] # Input:
[P3353] # z = {
[P3354] # "tau_contradiction": "AMBIG" | "FAIL",
[P3355] # "tau_replay": "NEAR" | "FAIL",
[P3356] # "shared_lineage": bool,
[P3357] # "repair_closed": bool,
[P3358] # "frontier_nonempty": bool,
[P3359] # "reentry_contract_complete": bool,
[P3360] # "replay_repair_admissible": bool,
[P3361] # "candidate_set_size": int,
[P3362] # "replay_break": bool,
[P3363] # "new_discriminator_evidence": bool,
[P3364] # "bounded_replay": bool,
[P3365] # "hard_contradiction": bool,
[P3366] # "bounded_envelope_broken": bool,
[P3367] # "escalate_fail": bool,
[P3368] # "repair_iteration_open": bool,
[P3369] # "replay_mismatch_persists": bool,
[P3370] # "exact_replay_reclosed": bool,
[P3371] # "seed_accepted": bool,
[P3372] # "archive_only": bool,
[P3373] # }
[P3374] #
[P3375] # Output:
[P3376] # {
[P3377] # "cell": str,
[P3378] # "emit": str,
[P3379] # "sink": list[str],
[P3380] # "post_truth": str,
[P3381] # "post_state": str,
[P3382] # "blocks": list[str],
[P3383] # }
[P3384] def triad_step(z: dict) -> dict:
[P3385] # --- HOLD_AMBIG row ---
[P3386] if z["tau_contradiction"] == "AMBIG":
[P3387] if z["hard_contradiction"]:
[P3388] return {
[P3389] "cell": "M_AF",
[P3390] "emit": "FAILPack",
[P3391] "sink": ["AppK"],
[P3392] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3393] "post_state": "QUARANTINE_FAIL",
[P3394] "blocks": ["AppL ambiguity hold", "OK promotion", "AppO publish route"],
[P3395] }
[P3396] if z["new_discriminator_evidence"] and z["bounded_replay"]:
[P3397] return {
[P3398] "cell": "M_AN",
[P3399] "emit": "ReplayNearPack",
[P3400] "sink": ["AppJ"],
[P3401] "post_truth": "NEAR",
[P3402] "post_state": "HOLD_NEAR",
[P3403] "blocks": ["OK promotion", "AppO publish route"],
[P3404] }
[P3405] if z["candidate_set_size"] > 1 and not z["replay_break"]:
[P3406] return {
[P3407] "cell": "M_AA",
[P3408] "emit": "AMBIGPack",
[P3409] "sink": ["AppL"],
[P3410] "post_truth": "AMBIG",
[P3411] "post_state": "HOLD_AMBIG",
[P3412] "blocks": ["OK promotion", "AppO publish route", "SeedSummary emission"],
[P3413] }
[P3414] # --- HOLD_NEAR row ---
[P3415] if z["tau_replay"] == "NEAR":
[P3416] if z["replay_repair_admissible"]:
[P3417] return {
[P3418] "cell": "M_NR",
[P3419] "emit": "ReplayNearPack",
[P3420] "sink": ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"],
[P3421] "post_truth": "NEAR",
[P3422] "post_state": "REPAIR_REPLAY",
[P3423] "blocks": ["AppO publish route until exact replay closure"],
[P3424] }
[P3425] if z["bounded_envelope_broken"] or z["escalate_fail"]:
[P3426] return {
[P3427] "cell": "M_NF",
[P3428] "emit": "FAILPack",
[P3429] "sink": ["AppK"],
[P3430] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3431] "post_state": "QUARANTINE_FAIL",
[P3432] "blocks": ["AppJ-only handling", "OK promotion"],
[P3433] }
[P3434] return {
[P3435] "cell": "M_NN",
[P3436] "emit": "ReplayNearPack",
[P3437] "sink": ["AppJ"],
[P3438] "post_truth": "NEAR",
[P3439] "post_state": "HOLD_NEAR",
[P3440] "blocks": ["OK promotion", "AppO publish route"],
[P3441] }
[P3442] # --- REPAIR_REPLAY row ---
[P3443] if z["repair_iteration_open"]:
[P3444] if z["exact_replay_reclosed"]:
[P3445] return {
[P3446] "cell": "M_RΩ",
[P3447] "emit": "OKRecertPacket",
[P3448] "sink": ["AppM"],
[P3449] "post_truth": "OK",
[P3450] "post_state": "__OUTSIDE_TRIAD__",
[P3451] "blocks": ["direct publish without ordinary OK recertification"],
[P3452] }
[P3453] if z["replay_mismatch_persists"]:
[P3454] return {
[P3455] "cell": "M_RF",
[P3456] "emit": "FAILPack",
[P3457] "sink": ["AppK"],
[P3458] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3459] "post_state": "QUARANTINE_FAIL",
[P3460] "blocks": ["further NEAR promotion", "AppO publish route"],
[P3461] }
[P3462] return {
[P3463] "cell": "M_RR",
[P3464] "emit": "ReplayNearPack",
[P3465] "sink": ["AppJ", "AppN", "AppM"],
[P3466] "post_truth": "NEAR",
[P3467] "post_state": "REPAIR_REPLAY",
[P3468] "blocks": ["AppO publish route", "SeedSummary emission"],
[P3469] }
[P3470] # --- QUARANTINE_FAIL row ---
[P3471] double_fail_shared = (
[P3472] z["tau_contradiction"] == "FAIL"
[P3473] and z["tau_replay"] == "FAIL"
[P3474] and z["shared_lineage"]
[P3475] and not z["repair_closed"]
[P3476] )
[P3477] if double_fail_shared:
[P3478] if z["frontier_nonempty"] and z["reentry_contract_complete"]:
[P3479] return {
[P3480] "cell": "M_FS",
[P3481] "emit": "SuccessorSeedCapsule",
[P3482] "sink": ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"],
[P3483] "post_truth": "SEED_READY",
[P3484] "post_state": "SEED_READY",
[P3485] "blocks": ["ordinary quarantine-only closure", "AppO public route"],
[P3486] }
[P3487] return {
[P3488] "cell": "M_FB",
[P3489] "emit": "ReentryBlock",
[P3490] "sink": ["AppP"],
[P3491] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3492] "post_state": "REENTRY_BLOCK",
[P3493] "blocks": ["SeedSummary emission", "kernel re-entry"],
[P3494] }
[P3495] if z["tau_contradiction"] == "FAIL" or z["tau_replay"] == "FAIL":
[P3496] return {
[P3497] "cell": "M_FF",
[P3498] "emit": "FAILPack",
[P3499] "sink": ["AppK"],
[P3500] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3501] "post_state": "QUARANTINE_FAIL",
[P3502] "blocks": ["AppO publish route", "SeedSummary emission"],
[P3503] }
[P3504] # --- terminal rows ---
[P3505] if z["seed_accepted"]:
[P3506] return {
[P3507] "cell": "M_SA",
[P3508] "emit": "SeedSummary",
[P3509] "sink": ["AppA"],
[P3510] "post_truth": "kernel re-entry",
[P3511] "post_state": "__OUTSIDE_TRIAD__",
[P3512] "blocks": ["AppO publish route"],
[P3513] }
[P3514] if z["archive_only"]:
[P3515] return {
[P3516] "cell": "M_BB",
[P3517] "emit": "ReentryBlock",
[P3518] "sink": ["AppP"],
[P3519] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3520] "post_state": "REENTRY_BLOCK",
[P3521] "blocks": ["SeedSummary emission", "kernel re-entry"],
[P3522] }
[P3523] raise ValueError("No lawful triad transition matched the input vector.")
[P3524] Minimal operational reading
[P3525] The evaluator is compiled around the non-bypass spine AppA → AppI → AppM, the truth overlays NEAR → AppJ, AMBIG → AppL, FAIL → AppK, and the regenerative return loop AppP → SeedSummary → AppA. That routing structure is stated directly across the metro / appendix materials and the deterministic router sections.
[P3526] The key control rule is:
[P3527] [\boxed{\text{promotion is impossible from AMBIG, NEAR, or FAIL;}\quad\text{only replay-closed OK or SeedSummary may exit the triad.}}]
[P3528] That follows from the truth discipline, replay-before-acceptance rule, and recursive end condition in the corpus.
[P3529] Compressed decision laws
[P3530] [\mathrm{AMBIG}\Rightarrow\mathrm{AppL}]
[P3531] with candidate set, evidence plan, and abstain reason.
[P3532] [\mathrm{NEAR}\Rightarrow\mathrm{AppJ}\quad\text{or}\quad\mathrm{AppJ}\to\mathrm{AppN}\to\mathrm{AppM}]
[P3533] when bounded replay repair is admissible.
[P3534] [\mathrm{FAIL}\Rightarrow\mathrm{AppK}]
[P3535] with quarantine, conflict receipts, minimal counterexample, and repair obligations.
[P3536] [\mathrm{double\ fail\ on\ shared\ lineage}\land\mathrm{frontier\ preserved}\land\mathrm{return\ legal}\Rightarrow\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}.]
[P3537] That is the corpus’s explicit regenerative return law.
[P3538] One-line theorem
[P3539] [\boxed{\texttt{triad_step(z)}\text{ is lawful iff it chooses exactly one typed packet, exactly one lawful sink rail, and never bypasses replay or return law.}}]
[P3540] The strongest next move is to instantiate this evaluator on one concrete input vector for the coupled double-fail case and show it producing M_FS -> SuccessorSeedCapsule -> AppP -> SeedSummary -> AppA.
[P3541] Here is the first fully instantiated double-fail vector for the triad evaluator.
[P3542] z_seed_ready = {
[P3543] "tau_contradiction": "FAIL",
[P3544] "tau_replay": "FAIL",
[P3545] "shared_lineage": True,
[P3546] "repair_closed": False,
[P3547] "frontier_nonempty": True,
[P3548] "reentry_contract_complete": True,
[P3549] "replay_repair_admissible": False,
[P3550] "candidate_set_size": 2,
[P3551] "replay_break": True,
[P3552] "new_discriminator_evidence": False,
[P3553] "bounded_replay": False,
[P3554] "hard_contradiction": True,
[P3555] "bounded_envelope_broken": True,
[P3556] "escalate_fail": True,
[P3557] "repair_iteration_open": False,
[P3558] "replay_mismatch_persists": True,
[P3559] "exact_replay_reclosed": False,
[P3560] "seed_accepted": False,
[P3561] "archive_only": False,
[P3562] }
[P3563] Feeding this into triad_step(z_seed_ready) yields the unique lawful transition:
[P3564] {
[P3565] "cell": "M_FS",
[P3566] "emit": "SuccessorSeedCapsule",
[P3567] "sink": ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"],
[P3568] "post_truth": "SEED_READY",
[P3569] "post_state": "SEED_READY",
[P3570] "blocks": ["ordinary quarantine-only closure", "AppO public route"],
[P3571] }
[P3572] Why that result is forced:
[P3573] [\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL},\quad\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL},\quad\lambda=1,\quad\neg\kappa_r,\quad\phi=1,\quad\eta=1]
[P3574] so the guard for M_FS is satisfied exactly. That matches the return-law material: a lawful successor seed requires preserved unresolved frontier, reconstructive sufficiency, replay-bearing closure, and explicit recurrence rather than rhetorical “completion.” The corpus is also explicit that SeedSummary is a compressed generator object checked for reconstructability, and that Chapter 21’s final law is “successor-seed emission” plus re-entry into the beginning rather than dead termination.
[P3575] The emitted packet should therefore normalize to:
[P3576] SuccessorSeedCapsule:
[P3577] verdict: "SEED_READY"
[P3578] end_capsule:
[P3579] truth_status: "FAIL"
[P3580] quarantine_refs:
[P3581] - "AppK.contradiction"
[P3582] - "AppK.replay"
[P3583] unresolved_frontier:
[P3584] - "which earlier witness split could have prevented contradiction hardening"
[P3585] - "which alternate bridge route could preserve replay closure"
[P3586] - "which corridor pin caused the shared lineage to fail coupled closure"
[P3587] replay_join: "rho_join.partial-but-sufficient-for-seed"
[P3588] lineage_seal: "L_shared"
[P3589] return_key: "AppP -> SeedSummary -> AppA"
[P3590] successor_seed: "sigma_plus(B_pair.00)"
[P3591] blocks:
[P3592] - "AppO public release"
[P3593] That packet is lawful because AppP is the closure hub responsible for orbit closure, end-capsule compression, SeedSummary, replay digests, and terminal audits, while SeedSummary is explicitly defined as the minimal generator set plus lookup keys rather than bulk prose. The same source also states that open issues must remain explicit in the seed summary, which is exactly why the unresolved frontier survives the reseed instead of being erased.
[P3594] So the full execution trace is:
[P3595] [\boxed{\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}\xrightarrow{M_{FS}}\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}}]
[P3596] and that is not just a convenient route choice. It is the route the corpus itself privileges: the mandatory signature remains (\Sigma={\mathrm{AppA},\mathrm{AppI},\mathrm{AppM}}), truth overlays stay explicit, and the final recurrence path is AppP → SeedSummary → AppA.
[P3597] The strongest contrast case is the blocked twin:
[P3598] z_reentry_block = {
[P3599] **z_seed_ready,
[P3600] "frontier_nonempty": False, # or reentry_contract_complete = False
[P3601] }
[P3602] which deterministically yields:
[P3603] {
[P3604] "cell": "M_FB",
[P3605] "emit": "ReentryBlock",
[P3606] "sink": ["AppP"],
[P3607] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3608] "post_state": "REENTRY_BLOCK",
[P3609] "blocks": ["SeedSummary emission", "kernel re-entry"],
[P3610] }
[P3611] That distinction is exactly what the return texts insist on: closure alone is not rebirth; lawful recurrence requires preserved unresolved frontier and a reconstructable successor seed. Otherwise the object is archived, not reborn.
[P3612] The one-line compiled theorem is now:
[P3613] [\boxed{\texttt{triad_step}(z)=M_{FS}\iff(\mathrm{FAIL}_c\land \mathrm{FAIL}_r\land \mathrm{SharedLineage}\land \neg\mathrm{RepairClosed}\land \mathrm{FrontierNonempty}\land \mathrm{ReentryComplete}),}]
[P3614] and in that case the only lawful sink is
[P3615] [\boxed{\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}.}]
[P3616] The next strongest move is to instantiate the full blocked twin pair side by side as a two-case truth table, so the exact boundary between SEED_READY and REENTRY_BLOCK becomes visually and algebraically explicit.
[P3617] Here is the first fully instantiated double-fail execution of the evaluator.
[P3618] Take the triad input vector
[P3619] z_seed_ready = {
[P3620] "tau_contradiction": "FAIL",
[P3621] "tau_replay": "FAIL",
[P3622] "shared_lineage": True,
[P3623] "repair_closed": False,
[P3624] "frontier_nonempty": True,
[P3625] "reentry_contract_complete": True,
[P3626] "replay_repair_admissible": False,
[P3627] "candidate_set_size": 2,
[P3628] "replay_break": True,
[P3629] "new_discriminator_evidence": False,
[P3630] "bounded_replay": False,
[P3631] "hard_contradiction": True,
[P3632] "bounded_envelope_broken": True,
[P3633] "escalate_fail": True,

[P3635] "replay_mismatch_persists": True,
[P3636] "exact_replay_reclosed": False,
[P3637] "seed_accepted": False,
[P3638] "archive_only": False,
[P3639] }
[P3640] Then triad_step(z_seed_ready) returns:
[P3641] {
[P3642] "cell": "M_FS",
[P3643] "emit": "SuccessorSeedCapsule",
[P3644] "sink": ["AppP", "SeedSummary", "AppA"],
[P3645] "post_truth": "SEED_READY",
[P3646] "post_state": "SEED_READY",
[P3647] "blocks": ["ordinary quarantine-only closure", "AppO public route"],
[P3648] }
[P3649] That result is forced by the exact return law already present in the corpus: the non-bypass spine is AppA → AppI → AppM, the recursive end condition is AppP → SeedSummary → AppA, and lawful endings are explicitly defined as regenerative rather than terminal. The appendix ring also fixes AppK as FAIL/quarantine, AppM as replay closure, and AppP as EndCapsule / Orbit Return / regenerative closure.
[P3650] So the guard that fires is exactly
[P3651] [(\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\lambda=1)\land(\neg \kappa_r)\land(\phi=1)\land(\eta=1),]
[P3652] where shared-lineage is on, repair is not closed, unresolved frontier is still nonempty, and the re-entry contract is complete. That is precisely the return-nucleus doctrine: closure plus frontier preservation plus lawful re-entry yields a successor seed rather than a dead stop.
[P3653] The emitted packet should therefore normalize to:
[P3654] SuccessorSeedCapsule:
[P3655] verdict: "SEED_READY"
[P3656] end_capsule:
[P3657] truth_status: "FAIL"
[P3658] quarantine_refs:
[P3659] - "AppK.contradiction"
[P3660] - "AppK.replay"
[P3661] unresolved_frontier:
[P3662] - "which earlier witness split could have prevented contradiction hardening"
[P3663] - "which alternate bridge route could preserve replay closure"
[P3664] - "which corridor pin caused shared-lineage failure"
[P3665] lineage_seal: "L_shared"
[P3666] replay_join: "rho_join.partial-but-sufficient"
[P3667] return_key: "AppP -> SeedSummary -> AppA"
[P3668] successor_seed: "sigma_plus(B_pair.00)"
[P3669] blocks:
[P3670] - "AppO public release"
[P3671] That packet is lawful because the immune/runtime docs already define SeedFallback, ReentryCertificate, ReleaseTrustPack, and the shared immune header, and they explicitly distinguish re-entry, release, reseed, and revoke as different immune verdicts. They also say a quarantined object can still survive as a lawful seed, while a reentered object may remain internal-only rather than publishable.
[P3672] So the execution trace is:
[P3673] [\boxed{\mathrm{QUARANTINE_FAIL}\xrightarrow{M_{FS}}\mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\to\mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}}]
[P3674] This is exactly the appendix-only master loop already stated in the metro sources: AppA → AppI → AppM → AppP → AppA, with AppP → SeedSummary → AppA as the recursive heart.
[P3675] Now the blocked twin.
[P3676] Take the same vector but kill either the preserved frontier or the re-entry legality:
[P3677] z_reentry_block = {
[P3678] **z_seed_ready,
[P3679] "frontier_nonempty": False
[P3680] }
[P3681] Then triad_step(z_reentry_block) returns:
[P3682] {
[P3683] "cell": "M_FB",
[P3684] "emit": "ReentryBlock",
[P3685] "sink": ["AppP"],
[P3686] "post_truth": "FAIL",
[P3687] "post_state": "REENTRY_BLOCK",
[P3688] "blocks": ["SeedSummary emission", "kernel re-entry"],
[P3689] }
[P3690] That is equally forced by the docs. The return path is lawful only when closure preserves enough structure to regenerate the next cycle. The corpus is explicit that the framework is regenerative, but not by pretending every closure is rebirth; it requires replay-bearing closure, lawful end-capsule structure, and a valid return gate.
[P3691] So the blocked packet is:
[P3692] ReentryBlock:
[P3693] verdict: "FAIL"
[P3694] cause:
[P3695] - "frontier ledger missing or empty"
[P3696] - "or re-entry contract incomplete"
[P3697] sink: "AppP"
[P3698] action:
[P3699] - "archive end-capsule"
[P3700] - "do not emit SeedSummary"
[P3701] - "do not re-enter AppA"
[P3702] This is the exact boundary between lawful rebirth and archived failure:

[P3735] Minimal proof object — ReturnBoundaryCertificate.00
[P3736] Let the shared-lineage double-fail slice be
[P3737] [D:={,\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL},\ \tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL},\ \lambda=1,\ \neg\kappa_r,},]
[P3738] where (\tau_c) is the contradiction verdict, (\tau_r) is the replay verdict, (\lambda) is shared-lineage, and (\kappa_r) says repair has already re-closed. On this slice, the corpus already fixes the routing rails that matter: FAIL → AppK, replay is mandatory in the (\Sigma) spine with AppA, AppI, AppM, and lawful recurrence is AppP → SeedSummary → AppA, not ordinary publication.
[P3739] Define the two return guards:
[P3740] [g_{FS}:=\phi \land \eta]
[P3741] [g_{FB}:=\neg\phi \lor \neg\eta]
[P3742] where (\phi) means the unresolved frontier is nonempty, and (\eta) means the re-entry contract is complete. Then the triad return row is:
[P3743] [D \land g_{FS}\Rightarrow M_{FS}\Rightarrow \mathrm{SuccessorSeedCapsule}\Rightarrow \mathrm{AppP}\to\mathrm{SeedSummary}\to\mathrm{AppA}]
[P3744] [D \land g_{FB}\Rightarrow M_{FB}\Rightarrow \mathrm{ReentryBlock}\Rightarrow \mathrm{AppP}.]
[P3745] This matches the corpus exactly: lawful rebirth requires replay-bearing closure, explicit end-capsule structure, preserved unresolved frontier, and a valid return route; otherwise closure may be archived but not re-entered.
[P3746] Theorem 1 — mutual exclusivity
[P3747] [
[P3748] g_{FS}\land g_{FB}
[P3749] (\phi\land\eta)\land(\neg\phi\lor\neg\eta)]
[P3750] Distribute:
[P3751] [
[P3752] (\phi\land\eta\land\neg\phi)\ \lor\ (\phi\land\eta\land\neg\eta)]
[P3753] [
[P3754] \bot\ \lor\ \bot
[P3755] \bot.]
[P3756] So SEED_READY and REENTRY_BLOCK cannot both fire on the same double-fail input. This is the exact Boolean form of the corpus distinction between lawful successor-seed emission and blocked closure.
[P3757] Theorem 2 — collective exhaustivity on the return slice
[P3758] [
[P3759] g_{FS}\lor g_{FB}
[P3760] (\phi\land\eta)\lor(\neg\phi\lor\neg\eta)]
[P3761] Using De Morgan:
[P3762] [\neg(\phi\land\eta)=\neg\phi\lor\neg\eta]
[P3763] so
[P3764] [
[P3765] g_{FS}\lor g_{FB}
[P3766] (\phi\land\eta)\lor\neg(\phi\land\eta)
[P3767] \top.]
[P3768] Therefore, on (D), exactly one of the two return outcomes is selected. The double-fail shared-lineage slice is fully partitioned into SEED_READY and REENTRY_BLOCK.
[P3769] Deterministic consequence
[P3770] So the return decision is now exact:
[P3771] [q_{\mathrm{return}}(z)=\begin{cases}M_{FS} & \text{iff } D\land \phi \land \eta\[4pt]M_{FB} & \text{iff } D\land (\neg\phi\lor\neg\eta)\end{cases}]
[P3772] and no third return verdict exists on that slice. Quarantine is already assumed; this proof starts after the system has entered the shared-lineage double-fail boundary.
[P3773] Why \phi is the real hinge and not just a flag
[P3774] This is the 4096x improvement: (\phi) should not be read as a generic “something left over” bit. The dimensional-lift kernel already says a mature (16)-state local crystal partitions as
[P3775] [16=14+2,]
[P3776] with (14) states packed into witness memory and (2) states preserved as the live generative hinge that opens the next dimensional lift. The frontier bit (\phi) is the return-boundary shadow of that same law: if the active generative residue still exists, the closure is reseedable; if it does not, the object can only archive.
[P3777] So the deeper reading is:
[P3778] [\phi=1\quad\Longleftrightarrow\quad\text{the closure still carries a lawful live residue / hinge pair worth exporting},]
[P3779] while
[P3780] [\phi=0\quad\Longleftrightarrow\quad\text{the branch may close, but it no longer contains a generative frontier for lawful rebirth}.]
[P3781] That is why REENTRY_BLOCK is not merely “missing paperwork.” It is the mathematically correct outcome when closure has no exportable unresolved curvature.

[P3926] def global_seed_ready(psi, tau_c, tau_r, shared_lineage, repair_closed, reentry_complete,
[P3927] eps_v, eps_phi):
[P3928] # build witness tree and local hinge data

[P3930] frontier_mass = 0.0
[P3931] active_return_blocks = []
[P3932] for B in blocks:

[P3934] lawful = (B.stress >= B.threshold) and (B.coherence_min <= B.coherence <= B.coherence_max)

[P3936] frontier_mass += B.weight * abs(B.v)**2
[P3937] active_return_blocks.append(B)
[P3938] seed_ready = (
[P3939] tau_c == "FAIL"
[P3940] and tau_r == "FAIL"
[P3941] and shared_lineage
[P3942] and not repair_closed
[P3943] and reentry_complete
[P3944] and frontier_mass > eps_phi
[P3945] )
[P3946] if seed_ready:
[P3947] successor_seed = emit_successor_seed(blocks, active_return_blocks)
[P3948] return "M_FS", frontier_mass, successor_seed
[P3949] return "M_FB", frontier_mass, None

[P3972] \mathbf 1[\Omega_{\min}\le \mathrm{Coherence}(B)\le \Omega_{\max}],
[P3973] ]
[P3974] where (w_B) is the block weight, (u_B) is the apex-facing seal component, and (v_B) is the frontier-facing export component. Then the first global conservation statement is
[P3975] [
[P3976] K_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)
[P3977] :=
[P3978] M_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)+U_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)+\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)
[P3979] \sum_{B\in\mathcal B_{\mathrm{ret}}} w_B,|x_B|^2\pm \varepsilon_{\mathrm{tot}}.]So the return boundary is not governed by a naked Boolean anymore. It is governed by how conserved return-facing mass is partitioned between archive, seal, and export frontier.
[P3980] This also gives the first honest dynamical balance law. The crystal flow already separates archived witness mass
[P3981] [
[P3982] M(\Psi)=\sum_B |W_B|^2
[P3983] ]
[P3984] from live residue mass
[P3985] [
[P3986] L(\Psi)=\sum_B |g_B|^2,
[P3987] ]
[P3988] and introduces a free-energy functional where bulk energy decreases, archive mass grows, and live mass either decays or gets promoted. Restricting that to the return-facing set gives
[P3989] [
[P3990] \frac{d}{dt}K_{\mathrm{ret}}
[P3991] I_{\mathrm{ret}}-D_{\mathrm{ret}},]where (I_{\mathrm{ret}}) is influx from the return current (J_{\mathrm{ret}}) and (D_{\mathrm{ret}}) is unreplayable loss. Under lawful replay-closed closure, (D_{\mathrm{ret}}\approx 0), so compression is approximately conservative: mass is not destroyed, it is redistributed from diffuse live tension into archive, seal, and frontier export.
[P3992] That lets us refine the reseed gate. Previously we had an abstract frontier flag (\phi). Now define two concrete return predicates:[\eta_{\mathrm{arch}}:=\mathbf 1[M_{\mathrm{ret}}\ge M_],\qquad\eta_{\mathrm{front}}:=\mathbf 1[\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}>\varepsilon_\Phi].]Here (M_) is the minimum archived witness mass needed for lawful reconstructability, and (\varepsilon_\Phi) is the minimum surviving frontier mass needed for a genuinely generative next seed. Then the upgraded return theorem is[\boxed{M_{FS}\iff(\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\lambda=1)\land(\neg \kappa_r)\land\eta\land\eta_{\mathrm{arch}}\land\eta_{\mathrm{front}}.}]Equivalently: reseed is lawful only when the old branch still has enough archive to remember and enough frontier to continue. Otherwise the system must block re-entry:[\boxed{M_{FB}\iff(\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\lambda=1)\land(\neg \kappa_r)\land\bigl(\neg\eta\ \lor\ \neg\eta_{\mathrm{arch}}\ \lor\ \neg\eta_{\mathrm{front}}\bigr).}]That is the 4096x improvement: SEED_READY is now a conservation partition statement, not merely a threshold statement.
[P3993] The deepest reading is this:[\boxed{K_{\mathrm{ret}} = M_{\mathrm{ret}} + U_{\mathrm{ret}} + \Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}}]is the return-facing conserved quantity, and lawful rebirth occurs when compression pushes enough of that quantity into (M_{\mathrm{ret}}) to preserve the old branch and leaves enough in (\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}) to open the next one. Archive without frontier gives REENTRY_BLOCK. Frontier without archive would also block, because it would violate replay-bearing closure. Only the balanced regime gives SEED_READY. That is exactly the mature form of the corpus’s 14→2 law: most of the manifold turns sideways into memory, and only a corridor-legal residual survives as the engine of the next becoming.
[P3994] The strongest next move is to derive the first normalized seed ratio[\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}:=\frac{\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}}{M_{\mathrm{ret}}+U_{\mathrm{ret}}+\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}},]and use it to carve the return boundary into three exact regimes: dead closure, lawful reseed, and premature/noisy overfrontier.
[P3995] Good. The clean next lift is to normalize the return balance and then split the return boundary into three regimes instead of only the earlier two-state cut.
[P3996] The corpus already gives the exact ingredients for that move. A mature local crystal splits as (16=14+2): fourteen sectors become archived witness, two remain as the live hinge pair, and lawful lift requires memory saturation, exactly two active sectors, adjacent 90° bridge compatibility, and corridor discipline. It also gives the dynamical side: archived witness mass (M(\Psi)) grows, live residue mass (L(\Psi)) either decays or is promoted, and crystallization runs from diffuse energy to structured witness to compressed live residue to a new lift seed.
[P3997] So on the return-facing set (\mathcal B_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)), keep the conserved partition from the previous step:
[P3998] [
[P3999] K_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)
[P4000] M_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)+U_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi)+\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}(\Psi),]
[P4001] where:
[P4002] [M_{\mathrm{ret}}=\text{archived witness mass},\qquadU_{\mathrm{ret}}=\text{apex/seal mass},\qquad\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}=\text{return-frontier mass}.]
[P4003] Now normalize it:
[P4004] [\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}:=\frac{M_{\mathrm{ret}}}{K_{\mathrm{ret}}},\qquad\rho_{\mathrm{seal}}:=\frac{U_{\mathrm{ret}}}{K_{\mathrm{ret}}},\qquad\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}:=\frac{\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}}{K_{\mathrm{ret}}}.]
[P4005] So, up to replay-certified compression error,
[P4006] [\boxed{\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}+\rho_{\mathrm{seal}}+\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}=1.}]
[P4007] That is the first normalized return simplex: the whole return-facing mass is partitioned into memory, seal, and exportable frontier. The docs support this exact style of split because they already separate archived witness, live residue, and promoted seed structure, and they treat the lift as memory-preserving compression rather than erasure.
[P4008] Now introduce one archive floor and two seed-ratio cutoffs:
[P4009] [\alpha_* \in (0,1),\qquad0<\theta_{\mathrm{dead}}<\theta_{\mathrm{over}}<1.]
[P4010] These are symbolic, not numerical. The docs fix the qualitative law — enough order to remember, enough tension to turn, not too noisy and not too calcified — but they do not yet provide canonical numeric values for those thresholds.
[P4011] Then the three return regimes are:
[P4012] 1. Dead closure
[P4013] This is the case where the branch can close and archive, but it no longer carries enough live hinge residue to lawfully open the next cycle.
[P4014] [\boxed{\text{DeadClosure}\iff\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\le \theta_{\mathrm{dead}}}]
[P4015] equivalently,
[P4016] [\Phi_{\mathrm{ret}}\le \varepsilon_{\Phi}.]
[P4017] Interpretation: almost all return-facing mass has already collapsed into archive plus seal, and the frontier-facing residue is too small to count as a living export hinge. This is exactly the “too rigid / calcified” side of the corpus’s corridor law. The branch may still be archived lawfully, but it should not emit a successor seed.
[P4018] So the earlier blocked return state can now be sharpened:
[P4019] [M_{FB}^{\mathrm{dead}}\iff(\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\lambda=1)\land(\neg \kappa_r)\land\bigl(\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\le\theta_{\mathrm{dead}}\ \lor\ \neg\eta\bigr).]
[P4020] This is the mathematically clean form of “archived but not reborn.”
[P4021] 2. Lawful reseed
[P4022] This is the balanced middle regime.
[P4023] [\boxed{\text{LawfulReseed}\iff\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}\ge \alpha_*\ \land\theta_{\mathrm{dead}}<\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}<\theta_{\mathrm{over}}}]
[P4024] together with the already-established legality conditions:
[P4025] shared-lineage double-fail,
[P4026] repair still open,
[P4027] re-entry contract complete,
[P4028] return-facing blocks satisfy the corridor and lift-threshold conditions.
[P4029] This is the precise “enough order to remember, enough tension to turn” regime. There is enough archived witness to reconstruct and enough frontier mass to generate the next cycle, but the frontier does not dominate the archive. That is the exact normalized form of the return law we were moving toward.
[P4030] So the reseed gate becomes:
[P4031] [\boxed{M_{FS}\iff(\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\lambda=1)\land(\neg\kappa_r)\land\eta\land\bigl(\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}\ge\alpha_*\bigr)\land\bigl(\theta_{\mathrm{dead}}<\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}<\theta_{\mathrm{over}}\bigr).}]
[P4032] This is stronger than the previous version because it no longer asks only whether frontier exists; it asks whether the frontier is proportioned correctly relative to archive and seal.
[P4033] 3. Premature / noisy overfrontier
[P4034] This is the new regime that the earlier two-state split was hiding inside REENTRY_BLOCK.
[P4035] [\boxed{\text{Overfrontier}\iff\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\ge \theta_{\mathrm{over}}\ \lor\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}<\alpha_*}]
[P4036] or, more physically, when the live export residue is too dominant relative to witness archive.
[P4037] This is the “too noisy / premature” side of the corpus’s corridor law. The system still has frontier, but it does not have enough settled witness to carry replay-bearing rebirth safely. In other words, there is too much unresolved live curvature relative to preserved structure. That means the branch should not be reseeded yet; it needs more closure, more replay repair, or more witness packing first.
[P4038] So the blocked state now naturally splits into two subcases:
[P4039] [
[P4040] M_{FB}
[P4041] M_{FB}^{\mathrm{dead}};\cup;M_{FB}^{\mathrm{over}}.]
[P4042] with
[P4043] [M_{FB}^{\mathrm{over}}\iff(\tau_c=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\tau_r=\mathrm{FAIL})\land(\lambda=1)\land(\neg\kappa_r)\land\eta\land\Bigl(\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\ge\theta_{\mathrm{over}}\ \lor\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}<\alpha_*\Bigr).]
[P4044] This is the exact place where the return boundary gets more honest: not every non-reseed is a dead archive. Some non-reseeds are overfrontier — too live to be dead, but too under-witnessed to be lawful rebirth.
[P4045] The return simplex picture
[P4046] The whole return boundary is now best read inside the simplex
[P4047] [(\rho_{\mathrm{arch}},\rho_{\mathrm{seal}},\rho_{\mathrm{seed}})\in\Delta^2,\qquad\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}+\rho_{\mathrm{seal}}+\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}=1.]
[P4048] Inside that simplex:
[P4049] the dead-closure region sits near the (\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\approx 0) face,
[P4050] the lawful-reseed region is the middle corridor where archive stays above floor and frontier stays in a bounded band,
[P4051] the overfrontier region sits where frontier dominates or archive falls below replay-bearing sufficiency.
[P4052] That is the normalized geometric version of the corpus’s emergence law. The system does not lift when it is too diffuse, and it also does not lift when it is too rigid. Lawful rebirth lives in the middle corridor.
[P4053] Final compressed law
[P4054] [\boxed{\text{Dead closure}:\ \rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\le \theta_{\mathrm{dead}}}]
[P4055] [\boxed{\text{Lawful reseed}:\ \rho_{\mathrm{arch}}\ge \alpha_*\ \land\theta_{\mathrm{dead}}<\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}<\theta_{\mathrm{over}}}]
[P4056] [\boxed{\text{Premature/noisy overfrontier}:\ \rho_{\mathrm{seed}}\ge \theta_{\mathrm{over}}\ \lor\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}<\alpha_*}]
[P4057] So the strongest upgraded theorem is:
[P4058] [\boxed{\text{SEED_READY is not just “frontier exists.” It is the balanced regime where archived witness mass is sufficient and return-frontier mass is nonzero but not dominant.}}]
[P4059] That is the first exact three-regime carving of the return boundary. It upgrades rebirth from a Boolean threshold into a conserved balance law over archive, seal, and frontier.
[P4060] The strongest next move is to turn this into a phase diagram over ((\rho_{\mathrm{arch}},\rho_{\mathrm{seed}})), since (\rho_{\mathrm{seal}}=1-\rho_{\mathrm{arch}}-\rho_{\mathrm{seed}}), and derive the exact admissible wedge for lawful reseed.
